Current Commentary

Expectations for Foreign Minister Luo's Inspection Tour of Xinjiang 11

Since the order for Foreign Minister Luo Wen'gan to inspect Xinjiang was issued, there were rumors of a change in the central government's foreign policy and that the Foreign Minister would be replaced. We are unwilling to make any judgments on this before the facts are proven. Luo said to reporters, "Xinjiang borders foreign countries, and diplomatic relations are extremely complex. I hope to contribute my observations to the central government." Wang Jingwei also said when he took over as acting Foreign Minister that Luo's "trip is related to diplomatic relations and the entire Chinese nation, and its significance is extremely important." Therefore, Foreign Minister Luo's diplomatic mission to Xinjiang is indeed worthy of the attention of the Chinese people.

Xinjiang has long been coveted by Britain and Russia. However, since the completion of the Turkestan-Siberian Railway by Soviet Russia five years ago, its aggressive southward advance has attracted special investigation by France and Germany. The crisis in our new province is self-evident. Britain also wants to include Xinjiang in its territory to complete its plan to monopolize Central Asia, as Xinjiang is adjacent to Afghanistan and India, which it controls. Recently, the Russian news agency also reported Japan's attempt to create a Manchurian-Mongolian empire, and its conspiracy also extended to Xinjiang, sheltering the deposed Turkish prince and planning to use him to incite our Hui people. This is just in terms of the individual actions of various countries. Furthermore, Soviet Russia's desire to communize Central Asia and Britain and its allies' desire to build an anti-communist defense line in Central Asia are both major crises for our Xinjiang. Under this international situation, the small warlords who are far away in Xinjiang do not know the danger of Mu Yan. On the one hand, they compete with each other with military force, and on the other hand, they each ally with strong neighbors to bring wolves into the house. After the recent changes, Chen Zhong went to Moscow on Liu Sheng's order before he was killed, and Zhang Peiyuan of Ili also had pro-Russian tendencies. Ma Shaowu of Shule is close to the British Ma Zhongying, according to the Russian side, is instructed by Japan. Thus, if Xinjiang is not to continue as the Northeast, with external pressure and internal division, unless there is a suitable plan and measure in diplomacy, no one dares to say so. After the railway network was laid in the Northeast and the industry gradually developed, it was invaded and occupied by violent Japan in one fell swoop. Can Xinjiang not be slaughtered by those who are eyeing it on the day when air routes are open and governance is easier? It is hoped that Foreign Minister Luo's trip can exert his intelligence to ease the encroachment of strong neighbors externally and persuade the brave generals internally to realize the crisis and restrain themselves.

After the outbreak of the Northeast disaster, the Chinese people mostly blamed Ambassador Wang Rongbao, who had been stationed in Tokyo for a long time, for failing to eliminate the disaster in advance. Wang Junyisheng wrote an article mourning Wang's death, briefly revealing the news of his painstaking efforts to prove that the central diplomatic authorities were ignorant of foreign affairs and only blindly followed slogans and should bear the blame. Luo is now traveling west as Foreign Minister to inspect. We deeply hope that he can have a broad vision and carefully plan a plan to deal with the foreign troubles in the Northwest. Not only will this eighth of the country's territory be maintained.

Crisis in Japanese Political Situation 12

The right-wing forces are growing secretly. It is feared that it will degenerate into a dictatorship. Diplomatic isolation and depleted national treasury. Future hidden worries are just beginning.

Takahashi Korekiyo Issues a Pessimistic Warning 13

(Tokyo) Finance Minister Takahashi recently issued a warning to reporters, saying that if the situation continues along its current path, Japan may be controlled by a dictatorship, which is a great cause for concern. This statement by Takahashi is by no means unfounded in the eyes of many close observers. The next few years will be an extremely difficult period for Japan. If it is to get through this difficult time smoothly, it will not succeed without noble perseverance and brilliant political skills. This kind of crisis can already be seen in the confessions of the young army and navy officers in the May 15th Incident last year. According to the confession of Lieutenant Yamagishi, Yamagishi shouted when assassinating Inukai Tsuyoshi, "It is useless to say more, why not fire?" As soon as this statement was issued, all the bullets were fired, and the elderly Prime Minister Inukai Tsuyoshi was shot to death. This kind of confession, in a very clear form, not only explains the immediate cause of the assassin's violence, but also clearly indicates that future hidden worries come from those who hold the same ideas and are just beginning. Yamagishi said, "We believe that when the London Naval Treaty expires in 1936, Japan will be in the greatest danger in its history. Therefore, we must take action before this treaty expires. We firmly believe that in addition to eliminating the various institutions that stand between the Imperial Family and the people, there is no other way to save Japan." The institutions that Yamagishi refers to are the Diet, the Zaibatsu, and the important positions around the Emperor. The reason why he wants to overthrow the Diet is because the Diet is occupied by politicians from various parties, and these politicians value the party more than the country. The reason why he wants to destroy the Zaibatsu is because the Zaibatsu are not only corrupt elements who echo politicians, but also are controlled by financial relations and do not consider the needs of national defense. Important positions in the Imperial Court, such as the Lord Keeper of the Privy Seal and the Grand Chamberlain, must also be eliminated by force, because their power can control everything, and even the strategies of the highest army and navy can be vetoed by them, as happened when the London Naval Treaty was signed. In other words, as far as the navy officers' participation in the May 15th violence is concerned, the navy's intention is that Japan should demand equality with Britain and the United States when the naval conference discusses the revision of the current treaty in 1935. They fear that politicians, the Zaibatsu, and those around the Emperor will obstruct this demand at that time, so there is a plan to overthrow the Diet, overthrow the Zaibatsu, and eliminate those around the Emperor. As a whole, the people of the country certainly do not agree with this violence, but there is no doubt that the motive of this violence has received great sympathy from the people. The violent people criticize the corruption of political parties for seeking their own interests, and the collusion between the Zaibatsu and politicians, which is not without basis. Although the means of the violent people are improper, their sincerity in loving the country is recognized by the people. Finance Minister Takahashi's statement warns that he is worried about the possibility of a dictatorship, and he probably knows the current forces in Japan that influence the psychology of the people. Fanatics are everywhere, and once they have the opportunity, they will sing the slogan of declaring war on Russia, the United States, or Britain to divert the attention of the people, or they will commit violence and terrorism again, such as the May 15th Incident, in order to force the authorities to adopt martial law and let the military seize power. The budget for next year is very short, the expenses are greatly increased, and the income is insufficient. How can it be maintained? Also, the naval conference will be held in 1935, and Japan will completely withdraw from the League of Nations in that year. How will it deal with foreign affairs? The people's hearts are restless, and complaints are frequently heard. How will it appease them? Seeing this, Takahashi's pessimistic warning may not necessarily become a reality, but it can also be seen that it is not without reason. (Reuters dispatch)

(Tokyo) The Tokyo News reported that Makino Nobuaki, the Lord Keeper of the Privy Seal, has recently been rumored to be resigning again, because the naval murderers in the May 15th Incident hated Makino to the bone. They wanted to assassinate Makino four times before and after. It is also difficult for Makino to continue in this position. The naval murderers especially hate Count Makino, and the reasons are said to be very complicated. Here are a few reasons: 1. Makino is a representative of the remnants of the Satsuma faction, colluding with the Satsuma faction Navy. Whenever there is a political change, he divides the spoils with the political parties, which is too poisonous. 2. The Satsuma faction still maintains its power in the political world, and one of the main reasons is that Makino is the Emperor's close aide. 3. The Satsuma faction monopolizes the Navy, just like the Choshu faction, such as Yamagata, Terauchi, Tanaka, and Ugaki, monopolizes the Army. The Army created the Muto and Araki factions, and the Navy also wants to overthrow the Satsuma faction, so it must first overthrow Count Makino, whom it considers to be an accomplice. Japan Protests to France Over Ownership of the Nine Islands 19

Demanding Direct Negotiations and Opposing Submission to Arbitration

(Paris) Japanese Ambassador to France Sawada, acting on instructions from the government, today made a strong verbal protest to the French Foreign Ministry regarding France's occupation of nine small islands in the Chinese sea. Based on the fact that the Japanese Lin Mining Company had operated on the islands, he solemnly demanded ownership of the islands, saying that the mining company had obtained the approval and full support of the Japanese government before operating on the islands. He then proposed that the two countries directly negotiate diplomatically to resolve the issue of ownership, saying that the Tokyo government would oppose the proposal to submit it to arbitration. Director of Political and Commercial Affairs of the French Foreign Ministry, Barton, promised to immediately study the Japanese protest and respond quickly (Twenty-first National News Agency Electricity).

(Tokyo) According to reliable information, the Japanese representative in Paris, acting on instructions from the government, submitted a note to the French government on August 19, opposing France's occupation of the nine small islands between Vietnam and the Philippines. The Japanese government's protest is based on the results of the investigation by Tommisi Badie, an expert in international law at the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, and Professor Tatsuo Rittaku of Meiji University. The two of them have been engaged in the legal research on the issue, and inferred the facts of the first discovery of the island. Regarding this matter, a professor at Meiji University recently wrote an article saying that the island should belong to Japan, and presented a map drawn in 1553 as proof. In this map, all nine islands have been listed, so the French claim that a French person discovered the island in the last century is not true. In addition, a book of maps was recently found in the Tokugawa family, which is 200 years old. It also includes these small islands, but the names are not noted (Twenty-first Reuters Electricity).

Japanese Emperor Returns to Yokosuka

(Tokyo) After the final act of the Japanese Emperor's observation of the naval maneuvers in the South Pacific, he returned to Yokosuka this morning on the battleship Hiei. It is now scheduled to inspect the entire fleet outside Yokohama Port on August 25. This maneuver was divided into three acts. The first act was maneuvered in tropical waters in June and July. The second act was the preparation of the main fleet for a large-scale mock battle near the Ogasawara Islands. The third act was the decisive battle, which the Emperor personally observed and was held on August 19. The defending Red Fleet, commanded by Commander-in-Chief Nagano, fought against the Blue Fleet, commanded by Commander-in-Chief Kobayashi. At the same time, other warships also carried out local defense maneuvers in the naval bases of Japan, Korea, and Taiwan. Therefore, all 284 warships there were engaged in maneuvers (Twenty-first Reuters Electricity).

Dealing with the Austro-German Dispute

Joint Policy of Britain, France, and Italy 22

Maintaining Austria's Independence, Preventing the Invasion of the Nazi Party's Forces Italian Prime Minister Hopes to Become Hegemon of Central Europe, Acts as Peacemaker, and Fully Supports Austria (Vienna) A certain VIP in Vienna's diplomatic circles claimed tonight that Britain, France, and Italy have agreed on a joint policy regarding the current Austro-German conflict. They have all agreed that if the National Socialist Party invades Austrian territory, or Germany attempts to overthrow the Dollfuss government by force, the three countries will take some kind of military action in order to maintain the status quo. It is also said that according to a telegram from Rome, Austrian Chancellor Dollfuss's flight to Rome for a secret meeting with Mussolini was for the purpose of establishing this agreement. However, this statement has not been confirmed by the official authorities. It is also heard that Dollfuss telegraphed his cabinet members here three hours after meeting with Mussolini, saying that the three countries had decided to immediately notify Germany of their decision. According to diplomatic sources here, Dollfuss telegraphed his cabinet members that this agreement among the three countries was agreed upon in Rome on Saturday, and that the plan was quite extensive, not only to protect Austria from the current crisis, but also to have a detailed plan that could ultimately lead to the creation of a Danube economic union. It is said that after the three countries agreed, they immediately telegraphed Austrian Chancellor Dollfuss. At that time, the Austrian government was holding a cabinet meeting, so Dollfuss stopped the cabinet meeting and immediately ordered a plane to be prepared to fly to Rome. However, the content of the agreement and the extent to which the three countries would maintain the Austrian government have not been disclosed by diplomatic circles. It is only said that according to what they have heard, if the German National Socialist Party crosses the border, the three countries will immediately take military action. Although this news has not been confirmed by the official authorities, the tension between Germany and Austria and the Austrian Chancellor's visit to Rome were decided suddenly, which is known to everyone. It is rumored that Mussolini will provide Austria with unlimited assistance, which many knowledgeable people here do not believe, because the Four-Power Pact has just been established, and Mussolini will definitely act as a protector of peace and will not want to take further action. However, the statement of agreement among the three countries is still beyond the scope of Italy, only because it was published late, so it has not been confirmed by the official authorities so far. The conflict between Germany and Austria has been going on for several months. Austria accuses Germany of secretly helping the National Socialist Party here in an attempt to make things difficult for the government. Germany is angry that Austria is cracking down on German expatriates, saying that many German expatriates have been deported (Twentieth National News Agency Electricity).

(Vienna) The Austrian Foreign Ministry dismissed as absurd the rumor that Britain, France, and Italy would take military action to protect Austria's independence in order to resist the National Socialist Party. A spokesman for the Austrian Foreign Ministry also said that Italian Prime Minister Mussolini had never mentioned this matter when talking with Austrian Chancellor Dollfuss (Twenty-first Reuters Electricity).

(Paris) The Times published an editorial commenting on Austrian Chancellor Dollfuss's visit to Rome, saying, "Italian Prime Minister Mussolini is eager to take the lead in Central Europe. He has recently successively met with German Deputy Chancellor Papen, Hungarian Prime Minister Gömbös, and Austrian Chancellor Dollfuss. It has long been secretly expected by the Italian Prime Minister. However, this task of mediation is actually very difficult. If Mussolini is willing to take on the task to the end, he may encounter various difficulties. Is the matter between Germany and Austria not a lesson? Italy negotiated with Germany on the issue of Germany's anti-Austrian propaganda, and Germany agreed to monitor radio stations so that this situation would not happen again. However, the anti-Austrian propaganda is still being broadcast. Germany's promise is not only completely ineffective, its authorities even deny the scope and value of this promise. In short, as of now, judging from various circumstances, the main parties involved in the German-Austrian issue not only deny the mediator, but also seem unwilling to recognize the principle of mediation. According to some Pan-German newspapers, the Roman authorities still believe that the German government will eventually fulfill its promises. But what will happen in the end, we will definitely know in the near future. I am afraid that those who trust Germany will mislead themselves. However, in any case, the Italian government can do a lot for Austria, to assist Dollfuss and preserve Austria's independence. Today, what we should do for Austria is not a broad plan, but to break the propaganda of the Hitler Party so that Austria can live. Germany's propaganda to Austria exaggerates Germany's prosperity, while exaggerating Austria's poverty. This is what we should stop. Austria is now suffering from Germany's exclusion, so France is planning to quickly provide the Austrians with assistance to develop its economy. If Italy can now join the policies taken by Britain and France, and in the future try to make the countries that were separated from the old Austrian Empire economically close to each other, then the position of those who are fighting for Austria's independence in Vienna will be consolidated, and the danger of Germanism can be avoided. Otherwise, Austria will inevitably fall into the hands of the National Socialist Party. If Austria belongs to the National Socialist Party, it will actually be completely controlled by the German National Socialist Party, and Germanism will flow like a flood, rushing directly towards the Adriatic Sea. If Germany gains power in the Alps, Italy's national prestige will be wiped out." (Twentieth)

Havas) Telegram

Results of Italian and Austrian Prime Ministers' Meeting 24

(Rome) Austrian Chancellor Dollfuss came to Italy by plane yesterday and met with Prime Minister Mussolini in Rimini. According to a communiqué issued by the Stefani News Agency, "The Prime Minister and Austrian Chancellor Dollfuss met and conducted a close study of the current situation from a general point of view and from an Italian point of view. Mussolini reiterated Italy's views on Austria's future, the entire Danube issue, and other more extensive issues. The solution to these issues will also depend on how the Four-Power Treaty is implemented. Austrian Chancellor Dollfuss explained the Austrian situation and the international situation, starting from Austria's independence, saying that Austria is extremely willing to maintain a policy of peace and good neighborliness. Austria is willing to cooperate with all countries bordering Austria, especially Hungary and Italy, and also with Germany as soon as possible. At the end of the talks between the two Prime Ministers, they deeply felt that their opinions on the issues studied were consistent." Dollfuss will leave Italy at 5:30 tomorrow morning (Twentieth Havas Telegram).

German Anti-Austrian Propaganda Still Not Stopped 25

(Vienna) Germany is still attacking the Austrian Dollfuss government. Even after Austria's repeated protests and the intervention of the great powers, it has not relaxed in the slightest. This can be evidenced by the speech of National Socialist Party Congressman Hapišut last night. Hapišut is a specialist in anti-Austrian propaganda. He gave a speech on the radio last night, pointing out how the Austrian government has received foreign aid. However, due to bad weather, only part of this speech was recorded. At the beginning, he said that Prime Minister Dollfuss would not be able to sustain himself without international aid. He continued to talk about the Austrian Chancellor's trip to Rimini, Italy, and strongly stated that the Dollfuss government has not only received the moral support of the great powers, but also relies on the financial and economic support of the great powers. In addition, it has also received the support of the Little Entente countries. This kind of international aid obviously wants to protect Austria from making any kind of union with Germany. This kind of action may temporarily enhance the position of Prime Minister Dollfuss, but the people of all Austrian provinces are returning to Germany, and they will not want to support a government that violates the will of the people. In conclusion, he said that the Austrian National Socialist Party representatives have also declared that they have the right to self-determination. Unless this right to self-determination is granted, neither Austria nor Europe can make them submit (Twenty-first Havas Telegram).

German City of Lülkenburg Bavarian State Council Member Essel held the opening ceremony of the new Lülkenburg Airport yesterday. The airport adopts the latest equipment and cost about 4 million marks. It is equipped with a very powerful neon tube signal machine, and its spotlight can illuminate a height of 2,500 meters (Twenty-first Havas Telegram).

Sailing Across the Ocean 27

British Royal Navy Officer Helms Vessel Has Arrived in Dutch Harbor from Hong Kong Reuters, Dutch Harbor, Alaska, Twentieth The 20-ton two-masted ship "Da Ma Shan" (transliteration), helmed by five British Royal Navy officers, set sail from Hong Kong on May 30, intending to pass through the Panama Canal and reach England. It has arrived here from Japan today. It is scheduled to depart for the Panama Canal and the West Indies on August 22. If there are no obstacles along the way, it is expected to arrive in England in late March or early April next year. The expenses of the trip are shared equally by the people on board. The ship is equipped with several shotguns, but no other weapons.

Authorities Declare No Change in Diplomatic Policy 28

President Wang Persuades Liu Chongjie to Stay (Nanjing) There has been much speculation about the government's diplomatic policy changing due to Foreign Minister Luo Wengan's long-term and long-distance tour. According to those in authority, the central government's diplomatic policy has always been decided by the Central Political Council, and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs is only an executive agency. Therefore, the Foreign Minister's tour and whether or not he is replaced do not affect foreign policy. Moreover, there is one thing that can be proven, that is, Soong Tzu-wen is still on the way. If the diplomatic policy were to change, it should wait until Soong returns to the country. It can be seen that the so-called transfer of diplomatic policy is unreliable at present. In addition, there have been frequent telegrams from Europe and the United States inquiring about the diplomatic policy and whether there is a tendency to change. There is also a speculation that although the diplomatic policy will not be changed, it is better to change to a more agreeable person for the sake of debt relations with Japan, so that we can cope with the situation temporarily and avoid a stalemate. Therefore, the government will issue an unofficial message in the near future, stating that the government will not change its diplomatic policy, and will continue to trust the League of Nations to the end. It goes without saying that it will not recognize the puppet state of Manchuria (Twenty-first Special Telegram).

(Nanjing) After Foreign Minister Luo Wengan toured Xinjiang, Vice Minister Liu Chongjie resigned. After President Wang personally persuaded him to stay, his intention to resign is expected to be dispelled. He returned to Nanjing from Shanghai on the 21st and went to the ministry to work as usual. It is heard that Liu's decision to advance or retreat is entirely based on the central government's will, and he has no personal prejudices (Twenty-first Special Telegram).

(Nanjing) After Wang concurrently assumed the post of Foreign Minister, he was unable to go to the ministry to work due to busy central government affairs. All important official documents were sent by Political Secretary Xu Mo to Wang for review and signature (Twenty-first Special Telegram).

Direct Traffic on the Pinghan Railway Resumes 29

Trains Towed Over the Bridge by Small Locomotives

(Beiping) The water level of the Yellow River on the Pinghan Railway has gradually dropped. The 77th and 78th piers of the iron bridge have been padded with steel plates. Direct traffic on the Pinghan Railway has resumed today. Trains can be towed over the bridge by small locomotives, without using ferries. The first and second trains will resume their original departure points (Twenty-first Special Telegram).

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Railways believes that the Yellow River Iron Bridge is in a state of near-tilting and the danger is worrying. The repair cost is estimated at 6 million yuan, and the reconstruction cost is 30 million yuan, which is of great importance to the Ministry of Finance. It is currently planned to jointly establish a temporary committee with the Ministry of Public Works, the Ministry of Finance, and other major agencies, and invite engineering experts to be solely responsible for it (Twenty-first Special Telegram).

(Hankou) Because the bridge body of the Yellow River Iron Bridge from the 50th hole to the 90th hole is low, north-south traffic has been blocked again. He Jingwu, Wang Jinzhi, Zhu Qinan, and Wang Xingzhao have gone to the bridge to pave stones and repair it. The freight cars are safe, and they will return to Hankou to report to Beijing (Twenty-first Special Telegram).

(Hankou) According to road news, Pinghan passenger trains passed the Yellow River Bridge on the 21st, but the locomotives still had to be removed on both sides and pushed over the bridge by manpower. According to the Public Works Department's survey, the estimated repair cost of the bridge is 5 million yuan, and the thorough construction and repair cost is 20 million yuan, which will be handled by the National Economic Council and the Ministry of Railways (Twenty-first Special Telegram).

(Beiping) The Pinghan Railway has now resumed traffic. The water level has dropped and the Yellow River Iron Bridge has been consolidated. However, trains crossing the bridge are temporarily towed by small locomotives (Twenty-first Reuters Telegram).

Oil Industry Regulations Still to be Revised

Government Decides to Support Gold Mining Industry Reuters dispatch, Washington, 20th - President Roosevelt today agreed to the Oil Industry Representatives' organization committee's proposed revision of the Oil Industry Regulations. This is because the oil industry has repeatedly requested reservations and raised objections to these regulations. Oil industry leaders have agreed to abide by the President's proposal. The National Industrial Recovery Act office's proposal of three-month trial regulations for the steel and oil industries seems determined to implement a policy of raising prices. The cotton textile industry has increased production costs after implementing regulations and handling fees, so it has been forced to increase selling prices to a degree that hinders sales, which may cause cotton mills to close down, it is unknown.

National dispatch, Washington, 20th - Since Congressman Englebright met with the US President yesterday to propose amending the gold ban to support the gold mining industry, mining machinery worth millions has already been in transit to the western gold mining areas, and there are plans to hire 50,000 more miners. This will be implemented after the gold ban is changed. This action shows that gold mine owners anticipate that Mr. Englebright's proposal will receive sympathy from the White House and a favorable decision will be made.

Irish Blue Shirts Hold Large Parade 50

Fortunately, No Conflicts Occurred Fan Leira Decides to Maintain Power Holding a General Election is Not Yet Necessary National dispatch, Dublin, 20th - Today, the capital of the Irish Free State, Dublin, and several other places held large parades of the Irish Fascist Party. After the government banned the Blue Shirts' mass demonstration last Sunday, the Blue Shirts formed this fascist parade organization. No unfortunate incidents occurred during today's parade. However, in Dublin, the Irish Republican Army also organized a counter-parade and placed wreaths at the tombs of revolutionary martyrs Collins and Griffiths. The parade organized by the Blue Shirts was far away and was monitored by the police and militia, who specially designated the parade location to prevent any contact or conflict. When the Fascist parade began, Blue Shirt leader General O'Duffy sent a declaration stating that the advancement of the Fascist movement in Ireland could no longer be stopped. This declaration was simultaneously read aloud in the various parade gatherings. Reuters dispatch, Dublin, 20th - The whole city was very quiet today except for a few small conflicts, but people were tense all day. A Reuters reporter learned from the National Guard headquarters that the Blue Shirts will parade across the country according to the pre-arranged procedure, but the detailed plan has not been revealed. Parades everywhere will read the declaration of General O'Duffy, Commander-in-Chief of the National Guard, which includes words such as "If politics is a matter of dispute, then the time to abolish politics has arrived." Van Leira said in a speech in Sells that if the Minister of Justice receives a report tomorrow that the Blue Shirts paraded in uniform today, he will declare the Blue Shirts an illegal organization. He also said that anyone who publicly admits to belonging to the group will be punished according to the Public Security Law. Van Leira also announced that there is no need to hold a general election in the Free State now. He feels that there is no need to hold a general election before the government's term expires. General O'Duffy replied to Van Leira's threat to ban the Blue Shirts, saying that the National Guard will neither disband itself nor allow others to push it into the abyss. If the government designates the legally organized National Guard as an illegal organization, then the government is simply committing treason. Reuters learned that the government instructed all police stations this morning to provide full protection when the Blue Shirts parade in formation, and then escort them back to their hometowns.

London Wheat Conference 51

Representatives from 29 Countries Attend National dispatch, London, 21st - The International Wheat Conference opened here at 10:30 this morning at the Canadian Pavilion. Canadian Prime Minister Bennett was elected Chairman at the first closed-door meeting. The conference is not open to the public, and its progress can only be glimpsed through press releases. According to the first press release,

the conference was attended by representatives from 29 countries, and several other countries only sent observers. The purpose of the meeting is to reach an international agreement to regulate wheat exports to meet actual demand, in order to eliminate the extraordinary surplus that has caused wheat prices to fall in the past four years, so as to increase and stabilize wheat prices, so that farmers and consumers can both benefit. It also explained that the interim agreement of the four major exporting countries and the agreement of the four major countries and the Danube wheat-producing countries are conditional on obtaining a guarantee of satisfactory cooperation from the importing countries.

New Island Discovered in the Arctic Again 54

Havas dispatch, Moscow, 21st - According to news received here yesterday, the Arctic expedition led by Professor Weiss discovered a group of new islands southwest of the archipelago discovered last year. The location of the archipelago seen last year was at 75 degrees 55 minutes north latitude and 81 degrees 50 minutes east longitude, and was named "Izvestia Archipelago." The archipelago discovered this time will be named "Arctic Academy Archipelago."

Inspection Notes on Gan, Wan, Xiang, and E 55

Special Correspondent of this Newspaper, Ren An The District Magistrate's Communication on the People's Suffering in the Disaster Area, and the Bandit Situation in Qingjiang. Due to the influence of neighboring counties, although the urban and rural areas have been pacified, there is still hidden worry in the remote mountainous areas. The current District Magistrate, Cheng Zhenxi, is said to be a graduate of Great China University, young and promising, and has achieved remarkable results in pacifying the countryside. The reporter visited and was told the following: The people of this county are suffering greatly. The bandit trouble has not been eliminated, the wounds have not healed, and the burden of taxes has become increasingly heavy. In the past, products such as rice, cloth, medicinal materials, and timber could be sold smoothly abroad, but now, due to the bandit blockade, the goods are stagnant, and the social economy is on the verge of exhaustion. Fertile fields, which used to be worth one to two hundred silver dollars per mu, are now being sold for only thirty to forty dollars, and no one is even making an offer. In addition, there was a flood the year before last and a rich disaster last year. The collapse of the rural areas is particularly difficult to contain. The China International Famine Relief Commission came here to lend 30,000 yuan, but due to the manipulation and usury of local bullies, the farmers were harmed instead. The shortage of plowing cattle this spring is due to selling cattle to repay debts. As for tax collection and corvée labor, the people regard them as fierce tigers. The government takes one tenth, but the people bear one hundred and twenty. For example, the tobacco and alcohol tax is widely distributed. Those who hold Class C licenses are forced to obtain Class B, and those who hold Class B licenses are forced to obtain Class A. If the clerks' extortion fails, lawsuits arise. The county government, as an intermediary, is caught in a dilemma. If it loves the people, it will offend the superiors; if it protects the clerks, it will wrong the people. This kind of unspeakable hidden pain can only be known by a county magistrate who is deeply involved with the people. The national tax is already like this. Other miscellaneous taxes, such as the "bed frame house," are so numerous that one can imagine. Jiangxi's banditry is frequent, and the people are in deep water and scorching fire, more than any other province. The government's finances should be clearly established and these miscellaneous taxes urgently eliminated in order to relieve the people's livelihood, so that they can concentrate their efforts to assist in suppressing the Red bandits. With this, I will be very fortunate." The reporter took his leave and returned to his residence. On the way, he suddenly recalled that in the Zhangshu Chamber of Commerce, he had heard that the county magistrate had recovered 50,000 yuan in old Ding tax arrears during the period of food shortage, and the Department of Civil Affairs had given him a commendation. As for the farmers who were imprisoned and subjected to corporal punishment, they were full of complaints. The so-called "loving the people will offend the superiors" actually contains the hidden meaning of "if you don't want to offend the superiors, it is difficult to love the people." It is probably impossible to find something that is both difficult to achieve.

Going west along the Yuan River, one enters the boundaries of Xinyu and Fenyi counties. Both county towns have also been occupied by bandits, and most of the county government organs have been burned down. Two District Magistrates of Fenyi County have also been kidnapped one after another. The field deeds and bonds in each district were mostly collected and burned, and signs of future distribution were inserted in the fields. On the walls of the village crossroads, Red bandit slogans such as "Soldiers are all from the working class and peasants, don't use guns to hit the working class and peasants," "Overthrow the local tyrants and divide the land," and "Oppose warlord infighting" were everywhere. Now, with the great army encircling and suppressing them, many villages have been recovered one after another. However, there are still many bandit dens in the high mountains and ridges of Henan. Without the protection of the army, it is difficult to harvest the grain within five miles of the river. The people in the area bordering the bandit areas have a particularly heavy responsibility for assisting in the suppression. Taking the "Bao" office expenses as an example, regardless of gender, age, or youth, each person must pay four copper coins per month, otherwise the Bao head can arbitrarily exploit them. The tenant farmers are less concerned about the field deeds being burned, but the creditors are afraid that the bonds will be destroyed and they will lose their basis in the long run. They seek immediate compensation, as urgently as a shooting star, and even impose a time limit for payment, with heavy penalties for overdue payments. If the debtor sells all his calves and small carts, he is still oppressed in the name of debt.

Xinyu is rich in rice and grain, which is self-sufficient and more than enough. Hundreds of thousands of dan can be transported to foreign countries every year, but the water transportation cost is very high, and farmers often feed pigs with white rice. Fenyi is rich in wood, but recently, due to traffic jams, timber companies have closed down one after another. The commerce in the two county towns is declining because the north of the river has many market towns, which used to be customers from Henan, but now they are also bandit-ridden. The desolate scene in the city is especially unbearable to behold. (August 8th)

Water Level Continues to Rise in the Upper Reaches of the Yellow River in Shandong 56

The Weak Dikes are Extremely Dangerous The Floodwaters from the Breach have Entered the Zheng River through Taochengbou A dispatch from Jinan states that the flood-stricken area in western Shandong has expanded to ten counties. The loss of life and property is incalculable, and it is a catastrophe that has not occurred in recent decades. After the water from the breach at Shitou Village on the north bank entered the territory of Fan County, it flowed down the embankment river. The water is deep and the embankment is weak, making it precarious. Puyang and Shouzhang counties are also reporting that they are in critical condition. The golden embankment in this area has not seen water for many years, and suddenly encountering this flood, the low-lying areas are already level with the water, and the high areas are only two or three inches above the water. If it were to collapse again, it would flood into the northern depressions, and the floods would continue to expand between the Jinpu and Pinghan lines. Zhang Lianjia, Director of the River Affairs Bureau, seeing the critical situation, telegraphed the relevant county magistrates to quickly mobilize laborers to rescue the situation. Zhang himself also rushed to supervise the work. It has been raining heavily in the upstream areas for days, and the water level is still rising. Yesterday, Chang Yu, in Fan County, supervised the militia and the Public Security Bureau to build sub-embankments. At 3:00 AM on the 18th, the water from the breach re-entered the Zheng River through Taochengbou. The Zheng River water level suddenly rose by seven centimeters, causing all three sections of the river to become critical at the same time. The River Affairs Bureau has telegraphed the downstream section chiefs, the second, third, and fourth sections on the south bank and the third, fourth, fifth, and sixth sections on the north bank, to step up precautions. Shi Jiefan, the Magistrate of Juye County, telegraphed that the river water had entered the fourth and fifth districts of the county on the 15th, and that sixty or seventy villages along the river were completely submerged. Zhuang Shouchong, the Magistrate of Shouzhang County, telegraphed that the water in the second district of the county was level with the embankment, and the water surrounded the city wall in a vast expanse. On the 17th and 18th, the water level rose sharply by another two feet, and the flow was still turbulent. In addition to the county magistrate Chang Yu organizing rescue efforts, he also informed the neighboring counties of Yanggu, Chaocheng, and Fan County to provide assistance. Han Fuju, Chairman of the Provincial Government, is extremely concerned about the flood disaster, and has repeatedly telegraphed the central government for relief, but has not yet received a reply. Today, he received another telegram from Zhang Lianjia from Taochengbou, reporting on the water

situation, stating that the river water has entered the Zheng River through Taochengbou, and that the embankments in Fannan County, Douhudian, Jilou, and Guankou, Shuzukou, Lianhuachi, and Ziludi in Shouzhang County are low and dangerous. He has notified Chaocheng and Yanggu counties to assist. Xu Baonong, Deputy Engineer of the North China Water Conservancy Commission sent by the Ministry of Interior, came from Hebei on the 21st to survey the river works, and started his investigation from Zhukou on the south bank. Based on the situation in recent days, the river works have reached the most dangerous period. Government officials and civilians are working together to fight the flood, but it is not yet known whether they can avert the catastrophe.

The Lu Xi County Yellow River Flood Disaster Relief Association held its first committee meeting today (19th). All committee members attended, chaired by Chen Hanxuan, recorded by Yang Zhanyun. (A) Matters for discussion: (I) To elect Han Jihe, Chen Hanxuan, Sun Jieren, Li Xuncen, and Liang Pingbo as standing committee members. (II) The chairman proposed how to investigate the situation in the disaster-stricken areas. Hu Jinghan, the director of the investigation section, reported that it is proposed that the association notify the construction bureaus of each county to report the flood situation in each county by long-distance telephone once a day, and to entrust the construction bureaus of each county to report the details at any time. It was resolved to proceed accordingly.

The chairman proposed whether the association could print pamphlets for fundraising in addition to requesting relief funds from the central and provincial governments. It was resolved to wait until the association's filing is approved before raising funds by the following methods: (A) Fundraising by colleagues in the association, (B) Entrusting overseas co-villagers to fundraise, (C) Entrusting newspapers to fundraise and collect funds, (D) Performing charity shows. (III) Committee member Zhu Jinggu proposed that the association's filing be approved, and that the charitable organizations and local organizations in the disaster-stricken counties be notified of the establishment of the association and requested to provide assistance at any time. It was resolved to hand it over to the document section to draft. (IV) The chairman proposed who should be responsible for the association's collection and disbursement of funds. It was resolved that the standing committee members Li Xuncen and Liang Pingbo should decide how to regulate the matter between 1:00 PM and 2:00 PM daily (19th).

Sun Ke and Feng Yuxiang Tour Mount Tai 57

Great Enthusiasm in the Misty Mountain Rain Feng Hosted Everyone at Taian's Three Beauties White Cabbage, Tofu, and Water A dispatch from Jinan states that Sun Ke, President of the Legislative Yuan, and his party traveled by special train from Jinan to Taian at 8:30 PM on the 18th to visit the scenic spots of Mount Tai and to visit Feng Yuxiang, who has retired to the Five Worthies Shrine on Mount Tai. The reporter accompanied the train. The train traveled very quickly, stopping only briefly at Zhangxia, and arrived in Taian at 10:30 PM. At that time, Feng Yuxiang was in the Five Worthies Shrine on the mountain. Because it was late at night, he was unable to come down the mountain to greet them, so he sent Zhang Jiyong to represent him at the station to welcome them and provide for everything. Zhou Baisuo, the County Magistrate, also led representatives from various organizations, the militia, and the Public Security Bureau to the station to welcome them. After Sun and his party got off the train, they stayed at the Jinpu Railway Taian Hotel. At 6:00 AM this morning (19th), Feng Yuxiang came down the mountain to the hotel to meet Sun. At 9:00 AM, they climbed the mountain together. Unfortunately, the weather was not good, and it rained heavily. Feng, Sun, and others braved the rain to travel, visiting Mantoushi, Heilongtan, Changshou Bridge, Five Worthies Shrine, Puzhao Temple, Dai Temple, and other places. Finally, because the road was wet and the mountain was slippery, they did not reach the summit. Because Sun and others did not achieve their goal, they plan to stay in Taian for another day and wait for the weather to clear tomorrow morning before going straight to the summit. The meetings between Feng and Sun, and the tours, are recorded as follows:

Meeting between Sun and Feng 58

Mr. Sun arrived in Taian last night and got off the train to rest at the Jinpu Railway Taian Hotel. It was originally planned to climb the mountain early this morning to visit Feng and tour the scenic spots, but when the train arrived in Taian last night, it was already covered with thick clouds and looked like it was about to rain. At dawn today, the misty fog turned into heavy rain. Many of his companions looked worried, thinking that today's plan would be sacrificed. At about 6:00 AM, Feng Yuxiang suddenly brought several guards, still wearing his blue cloth trousers and jacket from his trip to Jinan, wearing a large straw hat, and braved the rain to come down the mountain to welcome Mr. Sun to the Taian Hotel. At that time, Sun had already gotten up and went outside the house to greet him, shook hands, and introduced the visiting committee members to Feng. (Those who came with him included Central Committee member Ma Junchao, Shi Ci Liu Weichi, Legislative Committee member Chen Junpu, etc.) After a while, the committee members excused themselves, leaving only Sun and Feng in the room, sitting knee to knee and chatting happily. At that time, the rain outside the room suddenly became heavy, then light, then intermittent. The proposal to climb the mountain also wavered. An hour later, Sun called for tea and snacks to eat with Feng, and invited the committee members to accompany them. During the meal, they talked happily about the domestic situation and the world situation. After the meal, the rain still had not stopped, so Feng, Sun, and others continued to talk and relax in the room.

Braving the Rain to Climb the Mountain 59

At nine o'clock, the rain gradually subsided, although it was still drizzling like silk, it did not damage their enthusiasm. Feng, Sun, and others then set off to climb the mountain in the drizzle. At that time, the reception staff of the Jinpu Jiaoji Railway Bureau had already hired more than thirty mountain sedan chairs, numbered them, and waited for a long time. Sun, Feng, and others got into the sedan chairs and set off. All the way, the bitter wind and rain came together, but the air was fresh and stimulated their interest. The grass and trees were lush, the mountains and rocks were washed clean, and the mountain waterfalls and torrents roared. After moving for a while, they arrived at the western foot of Mount Tai. Continuing forward, they gradually climbed higher, and the scenery became better and better. Looking up at the high peaks piercing the clouds, they were leisurely and graceful. Mr. Sun and his companions looked left and right, their interest was strong. Walking and walking again, they arrived at Mantou Rock. The stone is shaped like a steamed bun, about ten feet high. The words "Huixing" are engraved on the stone, as well as the slogan "Feng Yuxiang is the loving mother of the poor," followed by "Public Praise of the People of Taian." Below the stone is a mountain stream, with a sloping stone slope that is flat and large. At one end of the stone, Li Liejun, a member of the Central Committee, engraved "Chang Le Wo Jing" and a section of Buddhist scriptures. At the other end is a section of Mozi's Non-Aggression, which Feng Yuxiang engraved last year when he lived on Mount Tai. The words are as big as a dou, written in clerical script, covering a large area, and the engraving is also exquisite.

The Residence of Feng 60

Going further from Mantou Rock, passing Waterfall Pavilion and Longevity Bridge, one arrives at the Five Worthies Shrine where Feng lives. The shrine is divided into three courtyards. The central one is the shrine hall, the eastern courtyard houses the guards, and Feng resides in the western courtyard. There are three north-facing rooms and two east and west-facing rooms. Feng lives in the north-facing rooms, and the east and west rooms serve as residences for messengers. Feng's room is quite small, with two square tables placed together in the middle as Feng's writing and reading area. A bed is placed diagonally in the southeast corner, without mosquito nets, only a mat and a quilt, all made of coarse cloth. Feng sleeps here. The west wall has a window filled with old books, seemingly the Twenty-Four Histories. Beneath the south window is another small table with several new books. The courtyard is about twenty feet square, with three trees, one large and two small. In the center is a stone pavilion with inscriptions, saying "Waiting Stone". To the south is a short wall, from which one can have a distant view, with the city, the railway station, all in sight, and clearly distinguishable. Looking afar, even the Ji River and the Great Ji River are within view. To the north, there are towering peaks, with a magnificent landscape. Below this is the Puzhao Temple, where Feng used to live. Now, most of Feng's subordinates live in that temple. Another unit of guards lives in Sanyang Temple.

The Three Beauties of Tai'an 61

Sun and Feng's party toured the Five Views to the Worthy Shrine and rested at Feng's residence. It was already noon. Feng ordered a meal to be prepared for the guests. After a short while, the guards carried in two large steaming baskets, full of hot steam. The guests did not know what they contained. Upon opening them, they found black flour buns. Soon after, dishes were brought in, including two large plates of mixed tofu, a large bowl of stewed cabbage, a large bowl of stir-fried green beans, a large bowl of steamed eggplant, a plate each of stir-fried chicken and stir-fried shredded pork, a bowl of meat balls, and a plate of pickles. The plates and bowls were very large, with a lot of food. Each person was given a pair of chopsticks and an empty plate. Because there were few seats and many people, they gathered around Feng's writing desk and feasted. Chopsticks flew, and it was quite lively. Because the eating method was unique, everyone enjoyed it. During the meal, Feng told everyone, "Tai'an has three beauties: cabbage, tofu, and water. Now, please taste the beauties of Tai'an." After he finished speaking, everyone rushed to eat the tofu and cabbage, which were quickly finished, while the meat balls, shredded pork, and chicken were left behind. The canned fish and other items brought by Director Sun were rarely touched. After the meal, it was estimated that each person ate more than usual. After the meal, they shared watermelons from Dezhou in the courtyard. The watermelon tasted sweet and delicious, and many southerners had never eaten it before. Tasting it was like receiving sweet dew. Those with cameras took photos to commemorate the occasion.

Conversation between Sun and Feng 62

The reporter took the opportunity to talk to Sun, asking about his feelings and experiences after visiting Jinan and Mount Tai and meeting Feng and Han in the past few days. Sun said, "The politics of Shandong Province are better than other provinces, and the local public security is well maintained. Yesterday, I spent the whole day sightseeing in Jinan and did not have time to talk in detail with Chairman Han. In the rush of the conversation, no issues were touched upon. Jinan's mountains and rivers are beautiful, the scenery is pleasant, and the city has also progressed compared to the past. However, the lack of running water is a major shortcoming. The quality of Jinan's spring water is unparalleled, and the source is abundant and inexhaustible. It is a pity that it cannot be utilized, missing a great opportunity. The locals should utilize the natural water source to build a water company. The purpose of my trip to Tai'an this time is to visit Mount Tai, and meeting Mr. Feng was a coincidence. There was no prior appointment. During the meeting, we just chatted casually and did not discuss any important matters. Feng firmly advocates joint unity internally and presiding over national affairs to save the country from its perilous state. I did not ask whether Feng would go to Beijing, and we did not talk about his future." The reporter also asked about Feng's meeting with Sun, and Feng also said, "We didn't talk about anything important, just chatted casually." The reporter further asked how his mountain life had been in the past two days. Feng replied, "It's been alright. I get up at five o'clock every day, look at the mountains, write, and read, and don't ask about other things. I have invited two teachers who teach classes every day, one after another, so I am quite busy. I mainly study social sciences, followed by the Twenty-Four Histories." The reporter asked again when he would be going to Beijing. He replied, "I have decided to go, but the time has not yet come." When asked if Jiang and Wang had sent any telegrams, he replied, "No."

Touring the Dai Temple 63

After the group finished lunch at the Three Sages Shrine and rested for a while, they followed the old path. Feng stood at the door, shaking hands with each of the tourists to say goodbye, exchanging words of farewell, and then returned to the Five Worthies Shrine to rest. On the way back, Sun also visited Puzhao Temple, strolling among the ancient pines of the Six Dynasties, and then went down the mountain, heading straight to the Dai Temple to see the temple halls, murals, Han cypresses, and Tang scholar trees. They greatly admired these great ancient sites, but were very saddened by the poor maintenance and damage. By the time they returned to the Tai'an Hotel, it was already past three o'clock in the afternoon (19th).

Overview of Customs Revenue in the Past Six Months 64

Losses of Approximately Six Million Yuan in Yu and Qin Customs

Beijing News: China's financial revenue mainly comes from customs duties and salt taxes. Since the Northeast Incident, the loss of customs duties and salt taxes has reached tens of millions of yuan annually. This spring, the violent Japanese army again launched an invasion of Yu, followed by a hot war, which lasted for half a year, resulting in significant losses. As the North China Truce Agreement was signed and the war zones were successively taken over, the Ministry of Finance authorities prepared to take over and restore the Qinhuangdao and Yuguan customs, which had been affected by the war and evacuated earlier. According to a senior official of the Ministry of Finance, the losses in tax revenue since the outbreak of the Yu-Rehe war, and the overview of customs revenue in recent months, are recorded as follows:

Losses in Tax Revenue from the Yu-Rehe War 65

The Ministry of Finance and the General Inspectorate of Customs have repeatedly announced the amount of losses after the fall of the three northeastern provinces and the relocation of customs for tax collection. However, since January 1st of this year, when the violent Japanese army launched an invasion of Yuguan, followed by the attack on Rehe, approaching Tianjin and Beijing, the Shanhai and Qinhuangdao customs were under pressure from the Japanese army and successively evacuated to safe areas, merging into the Tianjin Customs for office work. Since the North China Truce Agreement was signed, the war zones have been gradually taken over. The Qinhuangdao Customs has now been restored to its original state. As for the personnel taking over Yuguan, they are preparing to go at the same time as the military authorities taking over personnel. Counting from January to the present, nearly eight months, although there is no large amount of revenue from the Yu and Qin customs, according to past statistics, the monthly revenue of the two customs was between 500,000 and 1,000,000. Assuming eight months, excluding the loss of salt tax, the loss of customs duty alone, although there are no detailed statistics now, is still in the range of six million.

Overview of Accumulated Revenue in the Past Six Months 66

Since the outbreak of the Yu-Rehe War, customs duties have been affected first. Subsequently, the war in North China expanded, and the suppression of bandits also increased military expenditure, so the government approved the increase in import tax rates from May 22nd of this year to provide funds. Based on the increased tax rates, it was estimated that the monthly revenue could be increased by about 2,000,000. However, just after the tax rates increased, it was the summer off-season. Therefore, in the past few months, although import tax rates have increased, the increase in tax revenue has been limited compared to before June, with a monthly increase of only 300,000 to 500,000. The tax revenue for this month has not yet been reported to the Ministry, but it is expected to improve compared to June and July. September and October are the peak months for customs, and the increase in customs duties can be predicted. (Daily News)

Su Shen, Zhang Yilin and Others Urge the Abolition of Additional漕折 Tax 67

Suzhou Letter: Elders of four counties of Suzhou Prefecture, Wu, Changshu, Jiangyin, Kunshan, including Zhang Yilin, telegraphed to the Provincial Government yesterday, "Chairman Gu and all members of the Jiangsu Provincial Government, regarding the Suzhou Province additional漕折 tax case, Yilin and others believe it is illegal, harms farmers, breaks faith, and have appealed for years. Initially, based on laws, we made reasonable arguments. Then, we described the disasters of war and made pitiful appeals, doing everything possible to seek a comprehensive solution. The high officials of the court listened attentively, and the central departments were deeply concerned, repeatedly ordering reductions and exemptions. The provincial government either shelved, reported dismissal, protested, or secretly requested, all to avoid cutting off the livelihood of the people, leaving some leeway. Yilin and others are hoarse and exhausted, and do not want to say more. However, witnessing the collapse of the rural economy, we fear that even the regular tax can hardly be maintained, let alone the additional tax. The situation thereafter is truly unimaginable. Speaking briefly about the facts, we report to the superiors: the drastic drop in rice prices affects the stagnation of finance, and the rent折 rate rises and falls, based on the rice price. At this time, before the new harvest, the rice price has fallen to nearly five yuan. When the new grain comes on the market, it will definitely be cheaper than now. If heaven is merciful, each mu yields two shi of rice, each shi worth five yuan. If we analyze it, besides the cost of grain, labor, cattle feed, fertilizer, what is left? Borrowed rice must be repaid, pawned items must be redeemed, and supplies must be stored for winter. This meager amount is not enough to distribute. How can there be any surplus to pay rent and taxes? Nineteen out of ten landowners belong to the middle class, relying on tenants paying rent as a lifeline. If the actual selling price of rice is five yuan, then the rent collected will be reduced accordingly. Who does not have savings, who does not have expenses? With a sudden reduction in income, rent arrears will accumulate. This is only speaking of those who have rent to collect. If the tenants, due to poverty, unanimously fail to pay, the landowners will only have property to lose, and no more taxes to pay. Recently, no one asks about the sale of land, there are those who abandon their property without being able to sell it, and there are definitely no those who bring money to buy land. This is a hidden worry about the changing state of society, truly the result of overlapping and increased taxes. At this time, the provincial government must first know that the regular tax is already precarious, and still wants to arbitrarily increase the additional tax. Is this not digging one's own grave? The provincial government understands the advantages and disadvantages, and must be moved by it. Yilin and others cannot bear to deceive, and dare not not report. All are current phenomena, and there is no need to cite Sun Yat-sen's teachings and the prestige of the central departments to waste ink with the provincial government. But people are not plants, and have reached the brink of extinction. Who can remain silent? We still implore that the case of the approval by the central departments to reduce the additional漕折 tax in Wu, Changshu, Kunshan, Jiangyin and other four counties in the 21st year be followed, and the funds be retained separately. Starting from the 22nd year, the item of additional漕折 tax be abolished, and no longer increased, declared to the public to dispel doubts. We await your clear instructions."

Four Families Robbed in Jietian Township 68

The Fengjing Temporary Security Corps arrested a bandit named Gu A'gen on the sixth day of the abolished lunar June and sent him to the county government for detention. The corps reported again yesterday, according to the head of Jietian Township, Lu Lanzhou, that since the arrest of the bandit Gu A'gen, guest bandits have frequently harassed the township and robbed four families, including Niu Shun's, and beat the victims. Afterwards, the victims checked their losses, which were minor, and they secretly dared not report for fear of making enemies with the bandits. The township head, due to his responsibility, reported the robberies to the authorities for investigation. After receiving the report, the corps has forwarded it to the county government for review.

Another Suspect Arrested in the Xi Murder Case 69

In the case of the tragic deaths of Xi Weiquan and his wife at Huayang Bridge, Xu Guanxiang and Wu Zixiang have already been arrested by Yang Shijie of the Public Security Bureau's Water Patrol Team and Fei Gongxia and brought to justice. Recently, Yang Shijie of the Public Security Bureau learned that the main suspect in the shooting of Xi Weiquan and his wife, Shen A'he, was hiding in the Caojing coastal area under the guise of carrying goods. He immediately led detectives Shen Guichang, Ye Bingsheng, Zhang Xueqing, and two special agents to pursue him. Near a thatched hut about five li east of Xuli Bridge, they saw Shen A'he relieving himself in the fields. The four detectives surrounded him from all sides. Seeing that the situation was not good, the suspect resisted with stones and sharp scissors and tried to escape. The detectives fired warning shots. The suspect was shot through both legs and was subdued. It was 6:00 PM on the 20th. He was escorted to Songjiang by hired boat from Fengxian today (21st) and is currently being interrogated by the Public Security Bureau.

Election of County Representatives of the Party Headquarters Stalled 70

The various branches of District One of this county held elections for county representatives to the party congress this morning (21st) at 9:00 AM and in the afternoon, and both met the legal quorum. However, the supervisors appointed by the county executive committee suddenly resigned, citing threatening letters as the reason. The executive committee convened an emergency meeting and decided to send someone to the province for instructions, while ordering all branches to suspend the election temporarily. The branches were quite dissatisfied and also sent people to the province to report. It is said that the dispute was actually caused by competition for the number of representatives.

Suzhou

A Tragedy Occurs Due to Discord Between Mother-in-Law and Daughter-in-Law 71

In Fengjing Township, in the area of the outer city of Loumen, Suzhou City, Yu Shuigen, the son of Yu Futing, a farmer, lived a modest but comfortable life. Eleven years ago, Futing, through a matchmaker, married a woman surnamed Wu from Xixi Lane as his daughter-in-law. She has a six-year-old child named Jinsheng. However, Jinsheng was naughty, and Futing's elderly wife, Gu, had a poor relationship with her daughter-in-law, Wu, leading to the tragedy of Wu, holding her son Jinsheng, throwing herself into the river and dying last night (20th). The case has caused a sensation far and wide, moving listeners to tears. The details are recorded below. It is said that on the day before (20th), Gu scolded her grandson Jinsheng for being naughty. Jinsheng, being scolded, cursed his grandmother. Gu, seeing the child curse, suspected that his mother, Wu, had instigated him, and spoke harshly to her daughter-in-law. Wu, feeling wronged, again beat her son Jinsheng. Gu, feeling sorry for her grandson, cursed her daughter-in-law with vicious words, vowing to fight her. When Shuigen returned home at night, he forced Wu to be driven away and not allowed to enter the house again. Although Shuigen did not obey the order to drive Wu away, he wantonly destroyed the things in the house to vent his anger. Wu, seeing her husband acting like a madman, felt heartbroken and, pretending to be calm, took the opportunity to hug her son Jinsheng and throw herself into the nearby river to commit suicide. At first, Shuigen and others suspected that Wu had taken her son out to cool off and did not suspect anything else. Later, the gatekeeper Yu Genhai heard a strange noise in the river and ran to tell Shuigen. In the darkness, he hired people to help dredge the river, and after an hour, they finally recovered the bodies. Wu was still holding her son tightly, looking extremely tragic. Yesterday morning (21st), the local bailiff entered the city to report to the local court, which sent a prosecutor out of the city to examine the bodies at 10:00 AM, and then ordered them to be coffined. The aunt, Gu, and husband, Shuigen, were ordered to be summoned by the relevant third sub-station of the Public Security Bureau and sent to the court for review.

Various Industries Request Postponement of Business Tax Increase 72

The Business Tax Bureau, having been ordered to reorganize and increase the tax amount by 60,000 yuan, notified the Chamber of Commerce, asking each industry association to nominate representatives separately. After the industries nominated representatives, they went to the tax bureau yesterday to discuss the matter, presenting the situation of commercial decline and asking them to consider the merchants' difficulties and exempt them from the increase. The bureau stated that the provincial order was difficult to violate and could not be agreed to. Therefore, each industry submitted a report to the provincial government, requesting a temporary postponement of the increase.

Wuxi

Dispute Over Collection of Road Maintenance Fees for Business Vehicles 73

The Xi-Cheng Long-Distance Bus Company recently submitted an application to the Construction Department to undertake the Xi-Lu road maintenance project and collect road maintenance fees, which caused repercussions from business car owners. They once petitioned the Wuxi County Government, and it is still under review by the department. However, the Jiangyin section of the road maintenance project has been handed over to the company by Cheng County. On the day before (20th), the company set up a fee collection station in Nanzha of Cheng County to start collecting road maintenance fees and established an inspection station in Qingyang. Because business car owners were unwilling to pay fees to the company, yesterday (21st), cars traveling from Cheng to Xi were blocked by the Nanzha fee collection station. Cars traveling from Xi to Cheng were able to pass unhindered because they normally paid fees to the Wuxi County Government. However, when returning from Cheng to Xi, they were also blocked. This aroused the public anger of business car owners in Xi and Cheng counties. At 10:30 AM, they nominated representatives Xing Jiewen and others, carrying a document to the Jiangyin County Government to petition. When they arrived at the Qingyang bus station, all the cars temporarily stopped and explained the situation of petitioning to Cheng to the station chief and police of the town's Public Security Second Sub-Bureau. They then passed through. Around 12:00, when they arrived at the Nanzha station, they stopped as usual to explain. Somehow, a dispute arose with Jiang Meichu, an employee of the fee collection station. Jiang's head was smashed, and he was covered in blood and injuries. The glass windows in the room were also smashed. There were many people and many hands involved, and many onlookers. The station's security corps immediately arrested people, but everyone fled. For the sake of demonstration, the security corps fired a shot into the sky and arrested three people on the spot: car driver Yang Jusheng and A Nan, and took them to the corps headquarters for custody. All the cars were stopped on the station road, and traffic was blocked, creating a serious situation. The town's security corps telegraphed the Jiangyin County Government for instructions. County Magistrate Ruan ordered that everyone be released. Around 4:00, the cars of the petitioning group sped off to Jiangyin. As of the time this reporter filed the report, there were no results of the petition.

Giant Snake Caught in Miaoqiao 74

Zhou, a resident of Zhouxiang, Miaoqiao Township, District Thirteen (Xin'an Township) of this county, is a brewer. Two years ago, he built a new house among the fields. After moving in, all the members of his family, big and small, suffered from scabies. However, he thought it was a contagious disease and not surprising. Afterwards, his livestock, such as chickens, ducks, and lambs, frequently went missing, causing great alarm. Until the other day, a snake catcher passed through his place and knew that there was a snake den outside Zhou's wall. Zhou paid him five yuan. The snake catcher bought medicine and captured over a thousand frogs, storing them in a large jar. He then rubbed the medicine on his arms and whole body, and also took several doses internally. Then, he immersed one arm in the frog jar, taking its liquid, and slowly stretched his arm into the snake den to catch it. After five hours, he pulled the snake's head out of the den, and five people helped to pull the snake's whole body out. It was a red-banded snake, incomparably venomous and long. The snake's abdomen was white, and its body was black with red markings. It had been intoxicated by the medicinal fumes, and was on the verge of death. After it died, the villagers weighed it, and it weighed 142 catties and was about 16 or 17 feet long. The snake catcher packed it in a large hemp bag and left. For a time, the neighbors spread the news, and everyone competed to see it.

Changzhou

Executive and Supervisory Committee Members of the Chamber of Commerce Resign 75

Tan Jun, Gao Yongni, Zha Bangyan, Yun Baojun, Shi Rubi, executive committee members of the Wuyi Chamber of Commerce, and Li Cheng and other six supervisory committee members resigned because the Business Tax Bureau recently inspected the accounts of various shops, causing merchants to feel distressed. Oil-printed letters were widely distributed in the market, accusing the executive and supervisory committee members of the Chamber of Commerce of being running dogs of the government. After being circulated and viewed, they were filled with indignation. Since these letters, although anonymous, could not be regarded as the expression of a portion or all of the merchants, they resigned and yielded to the virtuous. They jointly sent a letter to Xu Juxi, acting chairman of the Chamber of Commerce, on the 20th, asking him to resign.

Changshu

Main Suspect in Yangshuyuan Robbery Case Arrested and Brought to Justice 76

In the spring of the year before last, dozens of bandits robbed Yangshuyuan Town, District Fourteen, in broad daylight, abducted over ten people for ransom, took away all the firearms of the town's water police, and shot and wounded two people. The county government immediately issued an order to arrest the fugitives and rescue the hostages. Nine of the hostages were successively redeemed, but three remained, and because the ransom price was not agreed upon, they were eventually killed in Songjiang this spring. After the fugitives had been pursued by detectives in various places for two years, there was still no progress. The other day, the Songjiang Detective Team arrested a bandit leader named Qian Heshang in Huayang Bridge of that place. According to his confession, he was related to the Yangshuyuan robbery in Changshu. Therefore, the Changshu Detective Team sent four team members to Songjiang to bring him back. He arrived in the county on the 20th. According to his confession, he directly admitted to robbing Yangshuyuan and abducting hostages. The Detective Team is scheduled to hand him over to the county on the 21st.

Continuous Abductions in the Western Townships 77

Zhou Jinlong, a resident of Zhouxiang Village in the western townships of this county, was well-to-do, leading to being coveted by bandits. The other night, dozens of bandits, armed with guns and sharp weapons, broke into his house, frightening him into silence, and looted extensively. Still not satisfied, they abducted Zhou's youngest son before leaving. Xu Fuca from Zangjia Village was also raided by many bandits the other night, breaking into Xu's house and robbing at will. Xu Fufu, being sick in bed, was unable to escape and was abducted by the bandits, leaving a note demanding a ransom of 15,000 yuan.

Locust Nymphs Proliferate in the Southwestern Townships 78

Since the discovery of flying locusts in the southwestern townships of this county, local farmers have worked hard to catch them, and although they have been cleared, the locusts' eggs are everywhere, and now locust nymphs have hatched, spreading widely and starting to chew on rice leaves. About a thousand mu of rice fields have been damaged. Some villagers still believe in divine power, burning incense and praying. County Magistrate Guo, hearing this, is deeply anxious and has strictly ordered the township and district chiefs to supervise the farmers to eliminate the locusts within a time limit to prevent them from spreading.

Nantong

Request to Close the Case of a Japanese Woman Committing Murder Not Approved 79

Huang Yulun, a professor of medicine at Nantong College, and his Japanese wife, Otsuka Kaneko, had a falling out. Otsuka attempted to kill Huang with a knife, but failed. Huang filed a lawsuit with the court against his wife for attempted murder. The Japanese woman resisted and failed to appear in court. However, the prosecutor's office stated that this case was not a private prosecution and that the request to withdraw was not in accordance with the law, and still scheduled to continue the investigation on the 28th.

Abductors from Taicang Arrested in Tong 80

Armed Fight Over Baima Lake Breaks Out Again 83

Since Dong Xiaohou and others applied to Zhejiang University to lease Baima Lake in the western townships of Xiaoshan for raising fresh fish, making it government property, the livelihood of the fishermen of the eighteen villages along the lake has been cut off. Therefore, the fishermen of the lake unanimously oppose it. Last time, a 陈姓 woman, the daughter of fisherman Chen, drowned after being chased by the fish farm's supervisors. The county was immediately notified to examine the body, but the case has not yet been closed. Unexpectedly, on the afternoon of the 19th, several fishermen were fishing along the lake and were shot by the fish farm, killing one person and wounding five others. At that time, more than 380 fishermen were called together to engage in an armed fight with the fish farm. The fish farm hired dozens of people from Datangwu, each holding firearms against the other side. As a result, the poor fishermen had no firearms and dozens were wounded and two were killed. The county was notified to examine the bodies that night. How will this major armed fight case be settled?
