Local News

Accidental Mishap During Ship Testing on the Chu You Warship Yesterday 85

The shell suddenly fired from the rear. Technician He Erkun's chest was pierced and he died on the spot. Section Chief Chen Daxian and Wang Yanshao were also injured. The naval cruiser Chu You accidentally fired shells during a test firing in Wusong yesterday. The shells unexpectedly fired from the rear, killing technician He Erkun on the spot. In addition, two others were injured. The reporters of the Huadong News Agency, upon hearing the news, made a special trip to investigate and recorded it as follows:

Overhaul Completed 86

The cruiser Chu You arrived in Shanghai previously and was docked at Gaochang Temple. The Jiangnan Shipyard sent craftsmen to overhaul it, which took a long time. It was then completed and entered the dock to inspect the bottom of the ship. The guns at the front and rear of the ship and the side guns were also inspected by personnel from the Naval Ordnance Department.

Trial Firing at Wusong 87

After the ship was repaired, it was ordered yesterday morning to sail from Gaochang Temple to the Sanjia Water area outside Wusongkou to test fire its cannons. The Ordnance Department specially dispatched Chen Daxian, the section chief of the inspection department, Lieutenant Technician He Erkun, and Wang Yanshao, three people, to accompany the ship to Wusong.

Sudden Disaster 88

After the ship arrived at the Wusongkou waters at noon, it began to test fire. Technician He Erkun personally performed the firing and had aimed accurately five times. On the sixth firing, Section Chief Chen Daxian advised He to rest a while and have a sergeant fire. However, He refused and continued to do it himself. When he put the shell into the chamber and pulled the trigger, the shell not only failed to shoot forward but instead shot out from the rear. At that moment, He was standing directly behind the cannon, and the shell penetrated his chest, causing profuse bleeding, and he died on the spot.

Two People Injured 89

Because the explosive force was very strong, in addition to He's death on the spot, Section Chief Chen Daxian, who was standing close by, was injured in the forehead, and Technician Wang Yanshao was injured in the back.

Report to Shanghai 90

The ship's captain, Fang Ying, immediately stopped firing after the accident and sailed the ship back, arriving at Gaochang Temple at about 3 p.m. (He's body was placed at the Wusong Command Post). Fang immediately went ashore to report to Chen Jiliang, the commander of the First Fleet stationed in Shanghai, and telegraphed Chen Shaokuan of the Naval Department in Nanjing.

Generous Compensation 91

He was 29 years old, from Minhou, Fujian Province. He graduated from the Mawei Naval Academy. He had just taken up this position. He was quite diligent in his work, and was highly praised by Li Shijia, the head of the department. Because he died in the line of duty this time, the Naval Department will give generous compensation. Section Chief Chen Daxian and Technician Wang Yanshao, who were injured, were bandaged and are not in serious condition.

Overseas Chinese in Mexico Appeal from the US to Shanghai 94

Describing the tragic situation of being expelled and crossing to the United States, Requesting assistance from all sectors. Mexico's expulsion of our overseas Chinese has been going on for years. The government has negotiated several times but has not been able to curb its ambition. Instead, it has intensified and become more ferocious. Although our domestic people are in deep water and fire, they still have a place to appeal, but overseas Chinese thousands of miles away have no way to cry for help. They only have a piece of paper to express their last breath of hope. The letter from the distressed overseas Chinese in Mexico is excerpted below.

Hiding in the Wilderness 95

Mexican politicians arbitrarily show their strength and barbarity, taking advantage of our domestic and foreign troubles and not having time to take care of overseas Chinese. They suddenly implemented anti-Chinese policies and indulged in their bestial nature. At first, they demanded bribes and made some perfunctory gestures, then they rigorously implemented the "90% rejection" rule, allowed the people to rob and loot, and then expelled the overseas Chinese, sealed their shops, and seized their business rights, causing tens of thousands of overseas Chinese to suddenly be displaced and suffering. Various forms of abuse have long been tearfully reported to all parties by various groups and individuals, and are believed to have been understood. At that time, the distressed overseas Chinese were forced to hide in the wilderness due to the burden of their families and the difficulty in raising travel expenses, seeking shelter from other international expatriates. Time passed, and two years passed in an instant.

Escaping Dangerously 96

Recently, due to long-term poverty and annoyance, they appealed to relatives and friends living in Mexico and abroad, asking for help. They gathered funds in various ways and prepared travel expenses. In the middle of this month, they took a train from the city of Shanba, Shan Province, intending to sneak into the United States through Nacari, hoping to be rescued and returned to their home country to live out their remaining years. Unexpectedly, at Nanheke Station in the Shansheng area along the way, eight or nine soldiers forcibly dragged us off the train, claiming that Chinese were not allowed to pass through Shansheng Province. The next morning, they used freight cars to load and drive us out of the Shansheng area. The distressed overseas Chinese were under violence and could not resist, so they had to bow their heads and sleep in the wilderness. Thinking about going forward was impossible, and retreating was nowhere to stay. Therefore, they disregarded death and life, took great risks, and led men and women, walking along the road for nine days and nights, arriving at Moshuyao Port in Shansheng Province.

Enduring Cold and Hunger 97

At that time, the weak were invaded by mountain winds and miasma, and four of them died one after another. The survivors were also sallow and emaciated, their feet were swollen like pillars, and the cries of children and wives echoed in the road. Seeing this tragic situation, it was difficult to bear. So they wept to the rural areas and sold everything they had, and then they were able to return from Moshuyao Port to Nacari Port. They crossed to the United States on the 22nd, and were detained for medical treatment for two days before they recovered. The US government claims to advocate humanity, although it did not give any abuse, but the food in prison, only a few things of thin porridge and bread for breakfast. It is difficult to satisfy hunger, and it must be extended to 5 pm before eating again. The body that has been looted has suffered from cold and hunger again. The time for begging is unknown, and there is nothing but a body. After a long voyage, the future is vast. If I return to my hometown, I am even more worried about the future.

Request for Relief 98

Moreover, among the companions, there are those who are neurologically disordered due to anti-Chinese agitation, there are seventy-year-old men who are dying, there are those who are shuffling and holding crutches. Those who are dying are suffering such a catastrophe. Life is unfortunate, and there is nothing more to add. Forced by hunger and cold, I do not avoid shame and solemnly tell the truth. I implore gentlemen from all over the world to show great compassion and generosity and provide relief to the distressed overseas Chinese when the time comes, then we will feel your great kindness without limit. I am tearful as I write, and I cannot express all my desires. I also hope you will take care of us. The distressed overseas Chinese Chen Guanji, Chen Mingqiu, Zhen Lunzan, Zhen Lunji, Wu Yuzhan, Wu Hongkou, Zhen Quanji, Chen Weilin, Li Junping, Li Jinglin, Li Zhiba, Li Jin, Li Haoxiang, [missing name] Ji, and twenty-two women and children in the Nucari prison in the United States kowtow together.

Adding Ships and Raising Funds 101

Liu said that the case of borrowing 400,000 pounds of Boxer Indemnity from the Sino-British to purchase new ships has now been signed. Santedang Property 102

The bureau has repeatedly negotiated with the French Church to renew the mortgage and extend the term, but the church said that the Paris headquarters had not authorized the Shanghai church, so it resolutely refused. Therefore, this amount must be paid off. In addition to the 40,000 taels that have already been paid, about 257,000 yuan still needs to be paid. Since the French Church does not allow the renewal of the mortgage, the bureau has to negotiate with bankers to borrow the money. The results of the negotiations are satisfactory, and this long-standing case can be fundamentally redeemed in a short period of time.

HSBC Loan 103

Liu Hongsheng also said that the two matters of borrowing money for shipbuilding and redeeming the Santedang property have finally been accomplished. Unexpectedly, the more important case of the HSBC Bank loan has arisen again. It was found that the HSBC loan was made when Fu Xiaoan was the director. The amount was 5 million taels, with five wharves as collateral. It was not repaid when it was due in the past, and it has been extended repeatedly to this day. Including the principal, interest, and additional borrowings, it has reached 7.7 million taels, which is equivalent to more than 10 million yuan in national currency. Now, HSBC suddenly sent a letter to the bureau, urging the performance of the mortgage and redemption of the loan, and indicating that it would no longer be extended. Since the bureau is currently borrowing money for shipbuilding, how can it have this huge amount of 10 million to pay off the creditors? But it cannot be ignored. The importance of the issue is paramount. In addition to reporting this matter to the board of directors for review, we may wait for Minister Song to return home before reporting it for handling. For the time being, there will be no statement. The Naval Department dispatched the Tongji warship, and Ouyang Ge, the captain of the Second Team of the Zhejiang Water Police, dispatched Commander Xu Shidan to assist in the suppression. The two sides fought fiercely for about two hours. The pirates were unable to resist. A group of pirates led by Xiang fled to the waters of Wentai. A group led by Li Guanwu fled to Huaihai and other places. Another group of pirates fled to the waters off Sheshan, and was severely attacked and repelled by Lu Gongren, the captain of the Ce Dian cruiser stationed there. They fled to Caozhuang in Ganyu, abandoned their boats and landed, and were intercepted by the police team stationed there. Yesterday, Director Zhang took a cruiser to inspect the ports and waters of Shengshan and Siqiao and ordered all the teams under his jurisdiction to strengthen defenses and prevent pirates from entering the country in order to maintain navigation.

Shanghai County Wealth Management Office Telegraphs to Request Exemption from Additional Grain Tax 104

The People are So Poor: The National Credit is Like That. The Shanghai County Local Wealth Management Office and others sent a quick mail telegram to the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Finance, and the Provincial Government, which said, "In previous years, an additional two yuan has been levied with the winter grain tax, and the people have appealed for exemption. The Ministry has approved an extension of one year, and it will not be continued. The province has approved that the case has been approved and should not be discussed." Now it is heard that when the winter grain tax is levied this year, there is also a proposal to levy an additional two yuan per stone, which has caused panic among the people, who all say that the people are so poor and the national credit is like that, year after year, it is an inexhaustible treasury. In recent years, the rural economy has been on the verge of bankruptcy, and scholars and officials from the government and the public are thinking about relief, and they also know that the people's livelihood is haggard and the foundation of the country is at stake. Those who are planning for the long-term interests of the country are taking the time to reduce taxes, let alone increase them. Moreover, this year's weather has been bad, and although it is not yet possible to predict whether it will be a bumper or lean year, the expenses of farmers and workers are already insufficient. This county has already cleared the land and collected the fees, and the grain tax is ordered to be limited. The people's resources are limited, and the endless demands are made, even ignoring the clear order of not exceeding 100 taxes per tax. Draining the pond to catch all the fish is unbearable for the people. The chairman is also a native of Jiangsu, and the people of Jiangnan have suffered from heavy taxes for a long time. The subordinates are under strict supervision from the elders, and they are anxious from morning to night, and it is difficult to sleep and eat. They know that the Ministry and the government hold the pain of injury, and they will never bear to add even the slightest burden to the remaining lives. Even if there are ministers who offer advice, they will surely silently eliminate it. However, in the midst of the people's panic, rumors are occasionally spread, and they tell each other in horror. As far as their eyes and ears can reach, they dare not block it from the upper levels. They should send a telegram to appeal and ask for mercy for the difficulties of the people and approve the cancellation of the proposal to increase the winter grain tax in order to maintain national credit and comfort the people. The Shanghai County Wealth Management Office Director Huang YunShen, Deputy Director Kang Yongnian, and Six District Chiefs Wu Shifang, etc. bow down.

Counterfeit and Damaging Domestic Goods 105

The Shanghai Citizens' Association for the Promotion of Domestic Goods notified Jia Jing Xin Sheng Society that the Shanghai Citizens' Association for the Promotion of Domestic Goods, such as Gongzu Sock Factory, Yingzhou Dyeing and Weaving Factory, etc., privately purchased Lama brand raw cotton from Dakang Textile Factory, changed it to Ren Zhong brand from Shenxin Fifth Factory, wove it into goods, and transported it to the market, passing it off as domestic goods in order to seek huge profits. Their actions were deceiving the public and undermining the domestic goods movement. The committee has decided to notify all members to refuse to purchase the products of these factories, and to send letters to the guilds of the knitting and cotton cloth industries to give them severe and effective punishment, and to send letters to the grocery industry guild and the First and Second Special Zone Citizens' Union to notify all stores in the city to pay attention to the products of these factories and refuse to promote them, so as to warn unscrupulous merchants. The original letter is recorded as follows:

Original Notice 106

(Omitted above) It was found that the newspapers of the 15th of this month published that Gongwa Sock Factory, Yingzhou, Dingxin, Junchang, Tonghe Dyeing and Weaving Factory, Sanyang, Jiuyi, Yukang Cotton Weaving Factory, Yongyuan Mercerizing Factory, Yixinghao, and ten other companies privately purchased Lama brand raw cotton from Dakang Textile Factory, changed it to Ren Zhong brand from Shenxin Fifth Factory, wove it into goods, and transported it to various ports. The Su-Zhe-Wan District Unified Tax Bureau has discovered the conspiracy and filed a lawsuit. It was found that these factories have lost their conscience and are greedy for profit. Such behavior is not only deceiving the public but also undermining the domestic goods movement. Our association is responsible and cannot remain silent. The 13th session of the 10th joint meeting of the executive and supervisory committees has decided to notify all members to refuse to trade with these factories, and to send letters to the guilds of the knitting and cotton cloth industries to give them the most severe and effective punishment, and to send letters to the grocery industry guild and the First and Second Special Zone Citizens' Union to notify all stores in the city to pay close attention to the products of these ten factories and refuse to promote them in order to warn unscrupulous merchants and maintain commercial reputation. The record is on file. In addition to notifying all members, we will send separate letters to inform you accordingly. I hope your association will take note of this and handle it, and I look forward to a reply. (Omitted below)

Factories' Defense 107

Also, Gongzu and other factories sent a letter to the association yesterday, saying, "Dear Sirs, we were surprised to read in the newspaper that your association has decided to notify the Citizens' Union of the First and Second Special Zones to inform all stores to refuse to use and crack down on the products of our factories. We have always purchased cotton yarn raw materials through brokers, and the tax bills are also attached to the goods. Our factories have no way of knowing whether they are genuine or fake. Later, the tax bureau discovered the alterations, and the responsibility should be borne by the handling broker. The procedures and books are not difficult to review. Moreover, the handling broker has also been detained. The truth will soon be revealed. The newspapers have misunderstood the facts and mistakenly pointed out that our factories made the alterations. Our factories have already applied to the guild of this industry to select staff to thoroughly investigate. Before the association has verified the matter, we are unwilling to make too many defenses. We hope that your association will not listen to one-sided statements and believe them, and decide to warn, so that the group that loves domestic goods will turn into an obstacle to the development of domestic goods. That would be fortunate. Sincerely, Shanghai Citizens' Association for the Promotion of Domestic Goods, Gongzu, Dingxin, Yingzhou, Tonghe, Jiuyi, Yukang, Junchang, Sanyang, and other factories."

Solar Eclipse Yesterday Afternoon 110

Yesterday at 1:10 pm, a solar eclipse began. It ended at 2:50 pm. However, it was only a partial eclipse, so the sunlight was still strong and there was no dim atmosphere. Because the citizens saw in the newspapers that the solar eclipse was in the middle of the day and the weather was clear yesterday, many people looked up, but many people could not see it because their eyes could not withstand the strong sunlight. The reporter looked up at the sun at 1:45 pm. At first, it was difficult to bear the dazzling light, but he still stared at it for a long time. Then he saw the lower end of the sun as if a piece of baked cake had been bitten off. In the end, he could not see much with his naked eyes. He closed his eyes and sat quietly to recover his eyesight. According to Dabaisha, the editor of scientific knowledge said that yesterday was only a partial eclipse. The total eclipse will have to wait until September 21, 1941 (the 30th year of the Republic of China), and only the central part of China will be able to see it. The rest of the provinces will only see it as a partial eclipse.

Report on the Activities of the Hua Dong People's National Salvation Army in Eastern Jilin 115

Requesting Assistance from All Circles in Shanghai

According to the Guowen News Agency, the Northeast Volunteer Army Support Association received a letter yesterday from Zhang Zhendong, a representative of the General Command of the Hua Dong People's National Salvation Army Allied Forces. The letter stated, "Zhendong was entrusted with a secret order from our General Commander Zhang this time, risking his life from the Jilin border to come here and request assistance from your association. He has personally presented the situation of our army's resistance against Japan and suppression of traitors, and has been understood and is awaiting orders. Our department has also dispatched Wang Lizhong, who brought with him a report of our army's victory in a major battle against the Japanese and puppet troops on July 22. We will now briefly present it to you all: The Japanese, because we have a formal organization, have repeatedly tried to destroy it. On July 22, they launched a large-scale attack on three routes. The first route attacked Baoqing, with a force of over 3,000, including over 600 Japanese soldiers and over 2,500 puppet troops, supported by three fighter planes. The second and third routes jointly attacked Boli, with a force of over 3,000 Japanese and puppet troops. General Commander Zhang personally led 8,000 elite troops to defend against the first route on the banks of the Qixing River, engaging in hand-to-hand combat for two days and nights, shooting down one plane. The enemy is now in disarray and retreating. Three battalions of puppet troops defected and revolted, killing Japanese soldiers in the chaos, causing more than a hundred Japanese soldiers to drown while desperately trying to escape. Only a dozen or so survived. Our army also suffered heavy casualties. We captured a large amount of Japanese weaponry, including the weaponry brought by the three defected battalions, not counting those, we obtained eighteen Type 74 field guns, sixteen mountain guns, more than ten machine guns, 362 rifles, 600,000 rounds of ammunition, 631 shells, seventeen cargo trucks, and thirty-eight large horse-drawn carts, all fully loaded with military supplies. However, the large carts were requisitioned from civilians by the enemy and have been returned to their original owners. The second route was defended by our Ru Youcai's army at Xinqiantun, and the third route was defended by our Chen Zongdai's army at Tuoyaozi Mountain, both of which were repelled by our army. As for the detailed battle situation, due to traffic blockades, we have not yet received a formal report, so we cannot describe it. The Japanese army, after suffering a major defeat, is urgently planning to attack again, and we are preparing countermeasures to resist. The reason why our army was victorious this time was because we had a slightly sufficient supply of bullets. The soldiers were confident and determined to kill the enemy, so the Japanese repeatedly attacked but failed to succeed. If Shanghai once again advocates for support, and the support arrives, the morale will be even more boosted, and the expulsion of the Japanese invaders and the recovery of lost territory will be just around the corner. If everyone holds a mentality of seeking temporary peace and ignores the patriotic heroes fighting desperately on the battlefield, then we can only do our best and, unable to form Shao Kang's army, are willing to emulate Tian Heng's five hundred followers. We believe that our countrymen are not lacking in understanding and will certainly not become slaves of a conquered nation.

Therefore, we repeatedly appeal and hope for your generous advice so that we may follow it."

This is a special copy for your information.

Shanghai Chamber of Commerce Replies to Hunan National Goods Museum: Lun Chang Products Are Not National Goods 119

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce sent a letter yesterday to the Hunan Provincial National Products Exhibition Hall, stating:

Regarding your letter of the 19th of this month, inquiring whether the Seven Roses brand satin cloth produced by the British firm Lun Chang Company is an imported product or a domestic product, which is difficult to identify, and requesting a reply after investigation, we have investigated the definition of foreign goods, which has two types: one is manufactured overseas and sold to China, and the other is manufactured in China by foreign capital based on the Treaty of Shimonoseki. Lun Chang is a British capital firm that manufactures in China, and of course belongs to the scope of foreign goods. Moreover, the outer packaging of the factory's products also has the words "British Lun Chang Factory," leaving no room for doubt.

This is addressed to the Hunan National Products Exhibition Hall.

Sichuan Groups Meeting to Discuss Relief Measures for Refugees in Northwestern Sichuan 127

The Sichuan Northwest Famine Relief Petition Group, the Sichuan Fellow Association, and the Sichuan Tongnanba Fellow Association in Shanghai invited leaders of Sichuan origin in Shanghai yesterday to discuss the practical measures to help the more than 2 million refugees from more than ten counties in northern Sichuan. Yang Shukan, Huang Fusheng, Gu Ao, Tan Yigong, Li Baibei, Wu Shan, Xia Lianggong, Lai Xinhui, Fan Chongshi, Liu Yuchuan, Song Yuqi, Li Jingyu, Yang Suichu, Shao Jigao, Li Xunfu, Huang Fogong, and other 30 people attended. First, the representatives of the petition group, Liu Zihe, Bao Heng, and Li Shenpei, reported in detail on the situation of the famine in northern Sichuan and the plight of the refugees fleeing and waiting for relief, as well as the process of petitioning the central party, government, and military authorities in Lushan and Nanjing, and their wishes for this trip to Shanghai. Then, Zhong Hangsu and Qiu Zhizhong, representatives of the Rotary Shanghai Fellow Association, reported that after receiving telegrams from Pan Wenhua, Chairman of the Chongqing Relief Committee, and representatives of the petition group, describing the disaster situation, they immediately decided on seven relief measures, six of which have now been implemented by the document department. Finally, Li Qingfan, a representative of the Tongnanba Fellow Association, reported on the previous petition to Beijing and the proposed fundraising process. After the reports of the various groups, Yang Shukan first expressed detailed and specific opinions, followed by Li Boshen, Gu Ao, Xia Lianggong, Tan Yigong, Lai Xinhui, and others, who expressed their opinions. As a result, it was decided that: 1. Yang Shukan and others of the Sichuan Central Committee in Shanghai would send a telegram to the central government, the Executive Yuan, and the Relief Committee to report the disaster situation and request a large amount of funds to provide relief to the refugees. 2. A telegram would be sent to Liu Xiang, the Sichuan Rehabilitation Governor, and the provincial government, requesting them to quickly prepare a large amount of funds to handle emergency relief. This money would be replenished when external funds were raised. 3. A telegram would be sent to the Chengdu and Chongqing Chambers of Commerce and the Relief Committee, requesting them to notify the chambers of commerce and relief committees of various counties to jointly raise large amounts of money to provide relief to the refugees, which would be reported to the government for reimbursement in the future. The two telegrams would be led by the Central Committee members, and the leaders from all walks of life who attended the meeting today could also freely co-sign, and Yang Shukan and Gu Ao were appointed to draft them. 4. Huang Fusheng, Xia Lianggong, Lai Xinhui, and others were appointed to be responsible for contacting Dai Jitao, Shi Qingyang, Lu Chao, and others of Sichuan origin in Beijing and Shanghai to come to Shanghai and hold a regular reception for various charitable organizations and philanthropists in the city. 5. Newspaper reporters would be invited to be hosted by the Petition Group, the Sichuan Fellow Association, and the Tongnanba Fellow Association in advance, so that the plight of the refugees could be fully publicized throughout the country. 6. Li Baishen, Tan Yigong, Zhong Hangsu, and Qiu Zhizhong were appointed to draft all the articles of association for the Sichuan Famine Relief Association. In the future, the Sichuan Central Committee members and fellow associations in Beijing and Shanghai would jointly contact various charitable organizations and philanthropists in the city to jointly organize a larger-scale charitable organization. After the discussion, the meeting adjourned.

Correction of Responsible Joint Transport Fee 128

The Ministry of Railways ordered the Railway Bureau to comply with the instructions issued yesterday by the Ministry of Railways, stating:

"It has been found that the responsible fee charged for responsible transportation should be 10% of the ordinary or special freight rate. For priority shipment, 30% should be added to the responsible freight rate. For the highest priority shipment, 60% should be added to the responsible freight rate. These are regulations in the General Rules and should not be arbitrarily increased or decreased. However, it has been found that the various railways have recently been charging the responsible fee for discounted goods that should be transported under the responsible transportation regulations according to their un-discounted ordinary freight rates, resulting in the responsible fee for these discounted goods exceeding the discount that should be added to the freight rate. This not only makes accounting difficult but also violates the provisions of the General Rules. In the future, when the railway charges the responsible fee for discounted goods that are eligible for responsible transportation, it should be calculated based on the freight rate after the discount, and should not be calculated based on the freight rate before the discount, in order to comply with the regulations. Please comply strictly with this order."

The Investigation Committee Replies to Pan Xulun 129

After doubts arose about the amount of donations to support the Northeast Volunteer Army, various circles organized a Committee for the Investigation of National Salvation Donations. There were rumors that the total amount of donations was no less than 20 to 30 million yuan. Accountant Pan Xulun paid close attention to the source of these rumors and sent a letter to the committee to inquire. Yesterday, the committee replied to Accountant Pan, stating:

"Mr. Xulun,

Regarding your letter of August 16, we respectfully acknowledge receipt. We understand that you inquired about the basis for the statement 'The total amount of donations from various ports at home and abroad to support the Northeast Volunteer Army should be no less than 20 to 30 million yuan.' This shows that you are paying close attention to the source and destination of the donations, and we deeply admire this. The basis for this statement is taken from newspaper advertisements and street discussions, but even an empty valley will echo a sound, so how can we know that there is no cause? Moreover, the transmission of rumors is originally one of the true public opinions of the people. Compared to the deceptive talk of so-called celebrities, how can they be equated? Therefore, taking it as evidence is not harmful. Moreover, the current issue is not about where the 20 to 30 million yuan came from, but whether there is any embezzlement, theft, or corruption of the donations. The purpose of the investigation is simply to investigate whether there is any malpractice in the donations. If there is malpractice, then greedy and lawless people cannot be allowed to roam free outside the law. If there is no malpractice, then those who are public-spirited, clean, and self-loving will be all the more clearly vindicated. Rumors and slanders cannot detract from their reputation in the slightest. Therefore, all fundraising organizations and individuals, if they believe that there is no malpractice as rumored, then they should open their doors at midnight and not be alarmed. They can present all their accounts and receipts one by one to dispel public doubts. This is what we have been hoping for day and night. At that time, our association would have no need to investigate, and the rumors and street discussions would be dispelled without being attacked. They will not be able to stir up social attention as they do today. Now, instead of focusing on this, they are focusing on the source of the 20 to 30 million yuan, which is putting the cart before the horse and making people greatly confused. Furthermore, the so-called 20 to 30 million yuan transmitted by street discussions, before the fundraisers have disproved this statement with facts, this suspected case will remain a pending case. Who can criticize taking it as evidence for reference? In short, the rise of the donation investigation movement is purely in response to public opinion and the suspicion of social benefactors about the receipt and expenditure of donations. If the fundraisers want to express their sincerity and integrity, openness and honesty, then there is no other way than to clearly and publicly announce their receipts, account books, and receipts of donations, and accept our association's investigation in a fair and impartial manner. To say that relying solely on clever words and the four words "so-called celebrities" can cover the ears of the world and block the mouths of millions of people is truly a foolish dream and should be stopped. There is still something that our association cannot help but say. Since you are one of the supervisory committee members of the Northeast Volunteer Army Support Association, and it is said that you are the one who keeps and audits the accounts of this organization, then your knowledge of the situation is more detailed and accurate than that of outsiders. Now that you criticize the rumors transmitted by street discussions as not worth taking, then why not tell us the reliable information that you know so that we can correct them and clarify right and wrong? This is something that our association cannot help but regret. If you say that you do not know everything, then we do not know what you are relying on to accuse us and criticize the street discussions as untrustworthy. Are you not being too harsh on our association and too lenient on others? Otherwise, you must know but deliberately not declare, so is your intention worthy of questioning? You will surely be held accountable for these two things. You are old and may not be clear about the dark secrets of the outside world, but your learning, morality, reputation, and personality have long been admired and noticed by the people of society. We hope that you will cherish yourself, adhere to 'doing things with conscience, not being confused by clever words and temptations, and not being a tool of demons and monsters, and working as a servant for tigers.' Then, not only will you personally gain the way to protect yourself wisely and end your reputation, but it will also be the fortune of social credit and the future of the nation. Our association adheres to the meaning of loving people with virtue and has high expectations for you, so we are not lenient in our words. Whether you know that we are guilty or know that we are right is up to you to think deeply and carefully, and to work together to save some face for the nation and the country. As we come to the end, our thoughts are racing and we cannot express all that we want to say. We only wish you good health.

Shanghai All Circles Investigation National Salvation Donations Committee

August 21st"

Dispute Between Merchants and Vendors on Jiangyin Street 134

Charity Group Replies to Representatives of Vendors

The Shanghai Charity Group replied to a letter from representatives of merchants and vendors on Jiangyin Street, stating:

"We are pleased to inform you that our group believes that the number of residents in the Lujiabang area has increased, and the Jiangyin Street vegetable market is increasingly crowded. In addition, standing in the open air, exposed to rain and sun, is inconvenient for both buyers and sellers. Therefore, we have demarcated three mu of land at the corner of Lujiabang Railway Station Road to build a vegetable market, containing 480 vegetable stalls. We first submitted a report to the Finance Bureau on December 16 of last year and obtained approval. The report and sketches were all understood. The bureau has submitted it to the 22nd standing meeting of the Vegetable Market Construction Committee, and approved the construction, requesting that detailed drawings be drawn and submitted to the Public Works Bureau to apply for a construction license and build it as soon as possible. This approval and drawings are kept on file. In May of this year, we advertised for bids for construction work. We reported to the Social Bureau and on the 15th, the Social Bureau sent personnel to supervise the opening of bids. On July 2nd, representatives of merchants and vendors on Jiangyin Street, including Du Jinbao, requested the cessation of the vegetable market construction. Our group sent a letter to the representatives, instructing them to request consideration from the authorities, and copied the original text to the Social Bureau for review. On July 17th, we received an approval from the Social Bureau, and the reports and copies were all understood, instructing us to still comply with the regulations and the group's original plan for the vegetable market construction. This approval and copies are kept on file. The representatives came to the group on the 11th and reiterated their previous request. Our group immediately copied the original letter and submitted it to the Finance Bureau for instructions. On July 26th, we received an approval from the Finance Bureau, and the reports and copies were all understood, stating that the bureau had decided to convene the 24th standing meeting of the Vegetable Market Construction Committee at 2:00 pm on the 31st of this month, and in addition to sending letters to the committee members to send personnel to attend, the group was requested to send responsible representatives to the bureau to attend the meeting. This approval and documents are kept on file. Our group sent staff member Ye Zhenquan to attend the meeting and stated the circumstances. On August 10th, several people claiming to be representatives of vendors on Jiangyin Street went to the home of Huang Xingjie, a director of our group, requesting the cancellation of the vegetable market construction on Railway Station Road. At 10:00 am on the 15th, representatives, including Du Jinbao, a hundred and seventy or eighty people, went to our group's office, asking our group to publicly agree to cancel the vegetable market. Our group agreed to reply after the board of directors deliberated. Unexpectedly, the representatives relied on the crowd and persisted. Later, members of the Public Security Bureau and the Social Bureau came to the group to mediate before they dispersed. On the 20th, our group's board of directors held a temporary meeting and decided that the matter concerned local public welfare and had been approved by the authorities. It was impossible to change it without authorization, and there was no reason to submit a request to the authorities to change the previous case. A letter should be sent to the representatives. Therefore, we have recorded the case for your review. In order to maintain the livelihood of the old stalls, our group allows them to bring the Finance Bureau's donation license to our group for registration. As of August 20th, 363 old stalls have been registered. The representatives who have registered include Du Jin, one for selling fish and one for selling vegetables, another new vegetable stall, Fan Gongliang's meat stall, Xu Chunhua's vegetable stall, Ling Heming's salt stall, Xie Liansheng's fish stall, and Yan Hongxiang's father, Wenyuan's, three fish stalls. Since the representatives used the name of maintaining the old stalls on Jiangyin Street to mobilize the public, there is no reason for them to register first. It is clear that others are impersonating them, and it should not be valid. However, fearing that the representatives are being used by others and blindly following, our group is giving them extra consideration and temporarily reserving their registration. If they can come to the group and declare repentance, they will be treated the same as other registered stallholders. Furthermore, our group will never charge rent beyond the prices stipulated by the authorities in the future. Please do not worry and please notify them on our behalf.

Addressed to all merchants and vendors on Jiangyin Street,

From the Shanghai Charity Group,

August 21st"

As Many As Ten Miserable Deaths 141

Eight Suicides :: Two Run Over by Vehicles

Six Women :: Four Men

Guo Wei, Prosecutor of the First Special District District Court Procuratorate, took a car to Feilun Road yesterday morning to examine the bodies of men and women, totaling ten.

The causes of death are described as follows: (1) Duan Liu, a 47-year-old woman from Henan Province. Her husband, Duan Yuqiao, works as a chef at the Liangyuan Restaurant on Guangxi Road. They live at No. 145 Zhangjiazhai, Aiwenyi Road. The other day, she had a quarrel with her cohabiting woman, Li Ni, over trivial matters. She thought about it and became resentful, and developed a sense of despair. She hanged herself alone in the bedroom. Her husband reported to the Jing'an Temple Police Station, which ordered detectives to take the body to the mortuary. (2) Gong Zhaodi, a 28-year-old woman, unmarried, lives at No. 792 Hartung Road. The other day, her grandmother, Gong Gu, slightly blamed her granddaughter for not bathing for five or six days. Unexpectedly, the woman felt resentful after being blamed and secretly took rat poison and committed suicide by swallowing it. Her mother, Gong Zhang, noticed it, but it was too late to save her. She died soon after. The Jing'an Temple Police Station also received a report and ordered detectives to take the body to the mortuary. Over One Hundred Shops on North Sichuan Road Request Postponement of House Tax Collection Again 142

Using House Tax from This Autumn to Next Spring

as Funds to Relieve War-Torn Areas and Revitalize the Market

(Central News Agency)

The Municipal Authorities have decided to start collecting house tax on North Sichuan Road yesterday, but shops there are still appealing for a postponement. Here is the petition to the Municipal Government and the Municipal Council jointly signed by Yifeng and 195 other shops:

Petition for Commercial Decline, Deepening Losses, Urgent Request to Postpone the Collection of House Tax Again to Maintain Commercial Hardship. We, the undersigned, submit that North Sichuan Road, as a road built beyond the concession, has suffered losses from war disasters, its vitality has been almost completely lost, and the market has been sluggish. Although we have endured pain to resume business, we have been losing money for more than a year, and the situation has become increasingly dire. Many have closed down, and we have repeatedly appealed for the postponement of the collection of house tax for several months, but no instructions have been received. Recently, we received a notice from the Finance Bureau stating that the house tax on North Sichuan Road is exempted for the summer and will be collected in the autumn. We are deeply frightened by this order. We have repeatedly explained the difficulties of the merchants regarding the house tax and requested that the collection be postponed until the market recovers slightly and the people's difficulties are alleviated, at which time we will pay the tax. We have detailed this in previous submissions. However, we believe that the municipal treasury is facing extraordinary deficits, and the general tax is an obligation that citizens should bear. How dare we continue to seek exemption? However, we merchants have been frugally trying to make ends meet since suffering from the war disaster. The disaster relief records for the entire district can be presented as evidence, and this is not an empty statement. At this time of lacking the magic touch to turn things into gold, and facing such dire straits, it is really impossible to crawl and rush to our deaths. We previously received a letter from the General Federation of Citizens stating that they would not send personnel to collect taxes again in the area beyond the concession until the issue is resolved. The original letter can be copied for your review. Now, after the merchants have gathered to discuss the matter, and after repeated exhortations from the Executive Committee members of the Municipal Council and the 25 District Associations, we have unanimously decided to request that the house tax from this autumn to next spring be used by our Municipal Government as funds to relieve the war-torn areas and exempt from collection to help revitalize the market. The regular collection after the summer will be the same. Citizens can gain real benefits, and our Municipal Government can fulfill its relief responsibilities to some extent. This will benefit both the government and the disaster situation. We hope that you will understand and approve. (The following is omitted).

Dismissed Postman Conspires with Friend to Steal Letters from Mailboxes 143

Tearing off the Stamps on the Letters for Profit

The Key Was Purchased from a Used Goods Stall

The Postal Bureau Dispatched Investigators to Investigate and Arrest

Kang Dingji, a local person residing at No. 36 Jiangyuan Lane in the South City, was formerly a postman with the number 620 at the post office. He was dismissed for some reason in August last year and has been unemployed ever since. Because he could not support his livelihood, he willingly committed crimes and conspired with his friend Wang Gengsheng from Ningbo to privately open the post office mailboxes placed on the side of the road at the intersection of Chongqing Road and Weihai Road, steal letters, and tear off the stamps on the letters to sell for profit. This kind of theft was not easily detected by the post office and was not easy to solve. Now, some senders feel that the letters they send are not received by the recipients and suspect that the post office is at fault. They have written to the Postmaster General to inquire, which has aroused the attention of the postal authorities. The bureau specially dispatched investigators Zhong Chaojun and Dai Qinglan to be responsible for the investigation. They knew that this malpractice was occurring at the mailboxes on the streets, so they went to various roads to investigate. At 8:45 PM the other night, they were investigating at the intersection of Chongqing Road and Weihai Road when they saw Wang Gengsheng opening the mailbox there. Zhong et al. saw him steal a letter from the mailbox and put it into his bag. He immediately ran away. They immediately shouted for his arrest and arrested him at the Zhabei Police Station. After questioning by the police chief, Wang confessed that Kang Dingji had instructed him to steal, and the police chief immediately sent detectives Su Yinggen and Ye Yushan, and Western Detective Chief Mo Hao, to arrest Kang. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the First Special District District Court, where Judge Wu Xiangzu conducted a preliminary hearing. Police Lawyer Zhang Shizhu stated the case and requested that the two defendants be punished for theft. Kang Dingji confessed that he could not find a job because he was unemployed, so he bought a key from a used goods stall and gave it to Wang to open the boxes and steal. However, the stolen mail could not be sold, so he had not done anything. Wang Gengsheng confessed that he was foolishly influenced by Kang to do this, and that the key had been discarded when he was arrested. Chinese and Western detectives also presented a stolen letter found on Wang, 36 letters found at Kang's home, and a number of stamps and photos attached to the letters to Judge Wu for review. Judge Wu ordered the defendants to be returned to custody and rescheduled the hearing.

Changes in the Oil Sales Cooperation of British, American, and Russian Oil Companies in China Again 145

British and American Oil Prices Drop, Guanghua Intends to Compete Again

Consulted with Russian Oil Everywhere Last Night on Methods

(French News Agency)

Mobil, Asiatic, and Texaco have recently been competing fiercely with the Guanghua Russian Oil and have been selling at a low price. The Russian Oil Everywhere Company products rely on their state-owned and domestic advantages and do not hesitate to depreciate prices to compete. For half a year, other British and American oil merchants have been greatly affected. In July, Mobil and the other three companies originally intended to join hands with Guanghua and no longer make unnecessary sacrifices in business. These four major oil companies each accounted for one share and were promoted equally. The Guanghua Oil Company, which distributes the Russian Oil Everywhere, has also obtained the tacit approval of the Russian Oil Everywhere Company, and it seems that there is a trend of moving towards the same goal. Therefore, in the recent month, the four major oil companies have uniformly priced gasoline at 80 cents, regardless of the high or low price. However, there was a change within the company yesterday. Mobil, Asiatic, and Texaco were originally on the same line, but yesterday Asiatic suddenly dropped the price of gasoline by 5 cents per gallon to 75 cents. Therefore, Guanghua felt that these oil merchants had abandoned the cooperation. Although the price was still 80 cents yesterday, it is expected that the price will also have to be lowered in the short term to greatly compete. Yesterday afternoon, reporters went to Guanghua to inquire. According to the staff of the gasoline department of the company, the current price of gasoline for our company is 80 cents, and the actual price is 68 cents, which is actually cheaper than British and American oil. Kerosene is 5 yuan and 70 cents per box. The sudden depreciation of the British and American oil companies today is due to internal changes in their companies. However, although our company is still marking the price of yesterday (the day before yesterday) at 80 cents today, it may also lower the price to compete with it. This matter is related to the market and is difficult to tell you in advance. At present, the gasoline portion is the only thing that Chinese oil merchants are competing for. Other kerosene is sold in the interior, and the prices vary according to the region, and it has not yet reached the point of competition. Today (ie yesterday), the chief of the gasoline department of our company, Mr. Li, and others will begin a meeting with the Oil Everywhere Company, so whether to depreciate prices or compete must be discussed and decided by the meeting. We will have accurate news tomorrow.

Opening of Two Railway Business Offices 150

The Director Issues a Letter to Colleagues Encouraging Hard Work and Scheduling a Supplementary Opening Ceremony to Host Guests from All Circles: The business offices of the Jinghu (Beijing-Shanghai) and Huhangyong (Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo) Railways held their opening ceremony at 8:00 AM yesterday, immediately commencing operations. Director Huang Boqiao, Chief of the Transportation Department Zheng Baozhao, and others attended the ceremony, issuing a letter to colleagues and outlining the preparation process. According to the manager of the business office, the official opening ceremony will be supplemented by a ceremony on September 1, after the completion of the North Station, inviting guests from all circles to visit and provide guidance. The details are recorded as follows:

Letter to Colleagues 151

Deputy Directors Huang Boqiao and Wu Shaozeng of the two railways issued a letter to colleagues, stating in brief: (1) It is not an innovation that railway business is conducted at stations, but the connection between stations and train yards is often on the periphery of a locality. Therefore, many railway operators in various countries set up separate offices in the prosperous centers of cities and convenient transportation locations to facilitate the close contact of merchants, such as the city business offices of railways in Europe and America and the city business offices of railways in Japan, all to fulfill this mission. Even in our country, the Jinpu (Tianjin-Pukou) Railway has established an office in Xiaguan, Nanjing, with the same purpose. Therefore, the trial operation of a business office in Shanghai by this railway is not an innovation. (2) It is an independent operation and a commercial experiment. We advocate that the operation of railways should be independent and commercialized. The current establishment of a business office is a gradual step towards independent operation and, in name and in fact, it should be absolutely commercialized. Stations have become bureaucratic offices that do not consider serving the public's convenience as the mission of the railway, and this can be said to be a deeply ingrained habit that is difficult to change. The establishment of the business office is a major test for us railway operators who have already awakened, to see whether we can demonstrate the spirit of independent operation and whether we can commercialize. (3) It still requires consistent efforts from within and without. The nature of the business office is only a branch of the business section of the Transportation Department. Therefore, the commercialization of the business office still depends on the commercialization of the Transportation Department itself. If the business office is very commercialized externally, but the related parts within the Transportation Department are not sufficient to support it, then the business office's solicitations to customers will say how convenient and reliable it is, but upon arrival at the station, the reality will be the opposite. This will cause the business office to lose credibility with the public and strike a major blow to the independent operation of the railway. However, the Transportation Department is only an important part of railway operation. Other departments and offices also have considerable relations. Therefore, at the same time, other departments and offices must make all efforts consistently to help independent operation and commercialization as the goal. (4) It is merely a matter within the scope of railway operation. Some may think that there are already many travel agencies operated by Chinese and foreign merchants in the country, and the establishment of a separate business office by this railway may be beyond the scope of the railway and may be suspected of competing for business. In fact, the railway, in order to facilitate its customers, establishes an office in a certain place to receive customer inquiries, issue passenger tickets, transport luggage and packages, and also handle special products to promote its passenger and freight transportation. It is just adding a reception point, an inquiry office, and a ticket office, which is still within the scope of its own business and is still something that it should do. As for the travel agencies, they are not limited to railways, but matters such as consignment of packages cannot be handled by travel agencies. Although their business types are similar, their natures are different and they can coexist without conflict. Moreover, for any business, more promoters mean more hope. Travel agencies are promoters for the railway. Therefore, the railway would never want to maintain its own business office and oppress travel agencies that help the railway. The above four points are what we urgently want our colleagues to understand. The preparation process of the business office will also be published in this issue of this journal and need not be repeated. As for the expenses of the business office, except for some special expenses during the start-up period, the remaining staff will be transferred from the original Transportation Department personnel, and no additional personnel will be added to fill the vacancies. The regular expenses will also be covered by the original budget of the Transportation Department and will not be added separately. However, the accounts of the business office will be listed separately in the future to see the profits and losses of the business. What we hope is that this small experiment can be gradually expanded so that the public can benefit more from its convenience, which will be to complete a part of our mission.

Preparation Process 152

The Railway Bureau published the preparation process, stating: After the plan to establish a business office for this railway was approved, the Transportation Department actively carried it out. It has been decided to officially start service today. The general situation of the preparation process is described as follows: (1) Personnel Selection: The establishment of a business office is unprecedented for this railway. Since there are no established rules to follow, everything must be carefully planned, and the future responsibilities are extremely important. Therefore, the selection of personnel is extremely important. They must be young, energetic, able to endure hardship, and have meticulous thinking in order to be suitable. The Transportation Department selected nine people from various departments and transferred them to serve in the business office. (2) Formulation of Rules and Regulations: Various service methods and detailed rules of work were discussed item by item by the managers and colleagues of the business office in advance. Meetings were held day and night and progressed quickly. Whenever difficult problems arose, discussions lasted for several hours in order to strive for thoroughness and appropriateness, so as to avoid many entanglements during implementation. The following have been formulated: (1) Measures for Receiving and Sending Luggage, (2) Detailed Rules for Receiving and Sending Luggage, (3) Relationship between the Business Office for Receiving and Sending Luggage and the Information Desk and Luggage Room, (4) Measures for Receiving and Sending Parcels, (5) Detailed Rules for Receiving and Sending Parcels, (6) Measures for Booking Hotels, (7) Hotel Booking Contract, (8) Measures for Purchasing Special Products, (9) Special Product Purchase Contract, and eight types of forms. (3)

Establishing Procedures: The work planned for the business office is extremely numerous. It is necessary to establish procedures and implement them step by step in order to achieve twice the result with half the effort. Therefore, the business office first handled the following five items: (1) Answering Inquiries, (2) Booking Sleeping Berths, (3) Issuing Passenger Tickets, (4) Receiving and Sending Luggage, (5) Booking Hotels. In the future, the following will be organized in sequence: Receiving and Sending Parcels, Purchasing Special Products, Touring and Traveling, Parcel Insurance, Collection of Freight, Receiving and Sending Small Goods, and Handling Freight Procedures. (4) Contacting Hotels: Booking hotels is very important for the needs of passengers. Staff were immediately sent to contact hotels in various places, and most of them have been completed. A total of 11 hotels have signed contracts, and other hotels are still in contact. (5) Contacting Cars: The number of cars needed for transporting luggage, parcels, and goods is quite large. Since this railway could not provide them in time, a special contract was signed with Xie Xing Public Automobile Transportation Company, which has experience in handling the receiving and sending of goods, to be responsible for transporting them. The exterior of each car is also marked with the words "Business Office" for identification. (6) Internal Arrangement: The internal arrangement of the business office was also carried out simultaneously. Two red lanterns are installed inside the glass showcase, one in English and one in Chinese, with the gold letters of various businesses written below. Machine charts, etc. are placed inside the showcase. (7) Publicity Work: Since the business office is a commercial organization, it is impossible not to pay attention to publicity during the initial establishment. The currently planned publicity methods are divided into five types: (1) Placing Advertisements, (2) Printing and Distributing Letters to Passengers on the Train, (3) Radio Broadcasting, (4) Pasting Posters at Various Stations, (5) Distributing Promotional Materials According to the Telephone Book.

New Evidence in the Box Corpse Case 154

The Police Offered a Reward Yesterday: In the box corpse case on the Japanese ship Shanghai Maru, after the culprit, Portuguese national Potto Lick Clementi As, and his accomplice brother, Joseph, were sent to the Portuguese Consulate, a preliminary hearing was held. Because the Consulate believed that it was necessary to wait for the evidence to be collected before proceeding with the trial process, the police have continued to collect evidence diligently in recent days, sparing no effort. It was successively discovered that the box cover containing the corpse was originally pasted with a piece of white paper with the name of the recipient, etc., which was first covered with blue carbon paper on the white paper, written with a pencil, and then coated with blue ink fountain pen writing. Now, the blue carbon paper has been found in Yifeng Lane. After checking, the handwriting on it is exactly the same as that on the box cover. At the same time, blood stains were found on the bedding and floor. The photo of the culprit obtained was also identified and confirmed by the landlord as the person who rented the room with the woman at the time and moved the boxes. Therefore, as of yesterday, the police had collected nine out of ten of the evidence. The only thing missing is the rickshaw puller who was hired at the time. Although the police have been investigating in all directions, there is still no trace of him. A reward was offered yesterday in the hope that the rickshaw puller who was hired at the time of the crime would report to the nearest police station to facilitate the proceedings. If there can be results within a few days, then all the evidence will be complete and formally submitted to the Portuguese Consulate. The Portuguese Consulate can then begin a public trial of the case.

Yuan Xiluo and Others Initiate the Reconstruction of the First Bridge in Pudong 155

Shanghai gentlemen Yuan Xiluo and others, in view of the fact that the First Bridge in Pudong, located at the border of their hometown of Nanzha, has been dilapidated due to years of disrepair and is becoming increasingly dangerous, and that if reconstruction is not urgently planned, it is feared that danger will befall, have jointly initiated fundraising for reconstruction with local gentry Shen Menglian, Zhang Xiaoliang, Zhang Yutian, Min Caizhang, Fu Zuoheng, Jiang Zhuoyun, etc., to benefit pedestrians and facilitate transportation. The recorded background is as follows: Weeping over the difficulty of wading across water, we sigh at the difficulty of traveling. Whipping stones into beams, we share the ambition to help people. Who will be the first to manage and initiate the project? We can rely on Zilai. Planning requires labor and care. We can rely on Bozhu. The First Bridge in our Nanzha Port in Nanhui County has been in disrepair for many years and is an important thoroughfare. The flying bridge is hidden, and the road reaches Fengxian. The water is vast, and boats travel to Xupu. Recalling the past, the flute-playing passerby rode on a long rainbow. To this day, the stone is broken, and the road is submerged. There are no birds or magpies to fill it. Although the beams are made of wood, people and horses still rest and neigh. Lacking the skill of turning lead into gold, we can only rely on the fox's armpit made of fur. Every time Xiluo and others look at the old site, they secretly wish to repair it. We are concerned about the difficulty of raising large sums of money and know that it is easy to lift with everyone's strength. We hope that kind men and faithful women will generously donate money, and we expect to accumulate tens of thousands to complete the silver ferry. Seeing the red railings and white boards in this place, it is not difficult to complete it in days. We predict that in the future, high-ranking officials will travel by horse-drawn carriages and together reach the road to heaven. All gentlemen should respond in unison. Pedestrians are already looking forward to it.

Five Key Culprits Behind the Gao Assassination Attempt Arrested 156

Xu Changrong Returns His Car License Plate: The Police Consider It a Key Clue: Since the attempted assassination of a Mr. Gao by assassins who organized a gang and opened fire near Huile Lane on Yunnan Road in late last month, the Laozha Police, which has jurisdiction over the area, has been doing its utmost to investigate. Until recently, it was discovered that the case was masterminded by local Xu Changrong (also known as Xu Tingyu). At the same time, it was also discovered that Xu and his accomplices in the case were hiding in Room 418 of the Shanghai Grand Hotel on Tianjin Road, plotting a second assassination attempt against Mr. Gao. Hua Chief Detective You A'gen, Detective Liu Junqing, Xie Shuiquan, Zhou Guirong, and others, after understanding the situation, armed themselves and rushed to the room silently late the night before. They took Xu and his accomplices Zhuang Haiquan, Chen Hanzhang from Guizhou, Du Ailin from Chongming (the chauffeur who instigated Xu), and Xie Furong from Suzhou, a total of five people, to the police station for detention. They were sent to the First Special District Court yesterday morning, where Judge Feng Shide interrogated them. According to the police lawyer, Ru Baoyi, who appeared in court, after investigating Xu's plans and the Mr. Gao whom they wanted to harm, the police are still continuing to investigate. Therefore, for the time being, no charges will be brought against them. He requested that they still be detained until the investigation is clarified before a decision is made. Judge Feng then asked Xu Changrong and others one by one about their names, ages, and places of origin. He then approved the police's request and ordered Xu and others to remain in detention and be interrogated again at a later date. However, it is heard that the police still have a key point to thoroughly investigate in this case. That is, when the case occurred, someone witnessed a car with the license plate 5070, which Xu had prepared, parked near the Dahua Hotel at the intersection of Xizang Road and Fuzhou Road, which was far from the scene of the incident. After several gunshots, the car hurriedly fled. Afterwards, someone based on this clue questioned Xu, but Xu stammered and said that he himself was lying at home at the time and the car had not driven out. After this questioning, the culprit realized the importance of the matter. In order to eliminate the evidence in advance, it is heard that he recently returned the car license plate. If this is true, it would be a major refutation of the case. Therefore, the police are currently making every effort to investigate this point.

Central Bank Inspection Report 157

The Central Bank issued its 170th report on the inspection of its issuance reserves, stating: In accordance with Article 15 of the Central Bank Regulations, the Bank is responsible for inspecting the reserve funds of the convertible notes it issues. On August 19, 1933, the 170th inspection was conducted at the Bank's Issuance Bureau, and the results are announced as follows: (A)

The total amount of convertible notes issued is 53,166,665 silver dollars, including 48,423,079 silver dollar notes and 4,743,586 fractional currency notes. The total amount of convertible note reserve funds is 53,166,665 silver dollars, including 43,512,665 silver dollars in cash reserve. This cash reserve includes 39,100,3962 dollars stored in the Bank's issuance treasury, 2,610,015 dollars stored in branches in various ports, 1,798,688 dollars stored in fellow banks, and 9,654,000 silver dollars in guarantee reserve. (B) The total amount of customs gold convertible notes issued is 417,269.40 dollars. The total amount of customs gold convertible note reserve funds is 417,269.40 dollars. This reserve fund includes 7,004.69 taels of standard gold, which at a fixed price of .5957 converts to 417,269.40 customs gold dollars. In accordance with Article 2 of the Central Bank Convertible Note Regulations, the cash reserve is 60% and the guarantee reserve is 40%. The results of this inspection show that the amount of cash exceeds 60% and the amount of guarantee is less than 40%, which is consistent with the regulations. This report is hereby made. August 19, 1933, Chairman of the Supervisory Committee of the Central Bank, Li Fuxun, Supervisors Wang Jingli, Bei Songsheng, Qin Runqing, Yu Qiaqing, Lin Kanghou, Xu Ji-.

Letters to the Editor 165

To the Editor,

Regarding the social news article published in your newspaper on the 20th of this month, titled "Kong Wanyu Commits Suicide by Poisoning Over Rent Dispute," which stated, "Kong delivered the payment to the court on August 1st, but the landlord was not notified by the court, leading to a grave mistake," the original terms of settlement in this case stipulated that the defendant should pay arrears of 101.7 yuan per installment at the end of April and May of this year. If the payments were not made on time, the plaintiff could request full execution of 202.14 yuan and demand that the defendant vacate the premises. The defendant failed to pay the rent by the deadline. On June 30th, the plaintiff filed a petition for eviction. This court issued a further summons. The defendant only paid 68 yuan on July 14th, and was instructed to clear the balance by July 26th, and was also urged to negotiate with the plaintiff to possibly avoid eviction. As the payment was not made by the deadline, on July 26th, the plaintiff and defendant were notified that the eviction order would be executed. The bailiff carried out the eviction on August 5th. Although the defendant paid 100 yuan on August 1st, he had repeatedly missed deadlines, and this could not stop the execution of the eviction order. This court handled this case without any errors. The information in your newspaper is inaccurate. Please correct it to avoid confusion.

Sincerely,

The Clerk's Office of the Shanghai First Special District Local Court of Jiangsu Province.

August 21st.

To the Editor,

Regarding the news item published in your newspaper on the 19th of this month, where a Central News Agency reporter inquired with the Land Bureau and published an article titled "City Land Price Tax to be Prepared for Collection," which contained the statement, "As for the commercial districts, there are still some agricultural lands, so it has been decided not to collect land price tax but to continue collecting agricultural tax," this is not in accordance with the facts. All land within the designated and announced commercial districts must be subject to land price tax. Only agricultural land outside the designated district boundaries will not be subject to price tax and will continue to be subject to agricultural tax. Therefore, we request that your newspaper make the necessary corrections.

Sincerely,

Shanghai Land Bureau

August 21, 1933.

Important Educational News

Japan Plans to Nationalize All Secondary School Textbooks 166

Eliminating the Competition and Sales Practices

(Dentsu, Tokyo, 21st) The Ministry of Education plans to nationalize or semi-nationalize all textbooks for various secondary schools, including middle schools, girls' schools, agricultural, industrial, and commercial schools, as is currently done with elementary school textbooks. The Ministry of Education will issue the textbooks or compile them under its supervision. Currently, this proposed reform is being studied in the library. Under the current secondary school textbook examination system, private publishers are free to compile textbooks and schools are free to use them. Recently, the number of applications for examination has increased dramatically. There are currently as many as 120 types of English textbooks and 80 types of Chinese textbooks. Due to competitive sales practices, significant advertising expenses are incurred. As a result, not only are the prices high, but it is also reported that there are often various collusions between sellers and school principals or teachers. The Ministry of Education plans to reduce textbook prices by 40% compared to current levels and eliminate the aforementioned malpractices. If the nationalization or semi-nationalization of textbooks is realized, it will have significant implications for the unification of secondary education.

Jiangxi Educational Administrative Conference Opens 168

Cheng Shi, Chairman, Delivers Opening Address

(Nanchang Correspondence) The Jiangxi Provincial Educational Administrative Conference was held in the auditorium of the Department of Education at 9:00 AM on the 16th. The chairman, Cheng Shi, Director of the Department of Education, presided over the meeting, which was attended by more than 300 people. After the opening ceremony, Cheng reported that the initiation of this conference was based on the instructions of Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, who believed that education in the bandit-affected areas of Jiangxi Province was of great importance. He ordered a conference of secondary school principals to be held. He felt it was better to expand the scope and hold an educational administrative conference to seek overall solutions. The proposals are divided into seven groups, each with one or two core proposals submitted by the department for centralized discussion. There were 60 proposals from members, divided as follows: 18 from the Local Educational Administration Group, 7 from the Bandit-Affected Area Education Group, 7 from the Health Education Group, 5 from the Youth Training Group, 9 from the Vocational Education Group, 12 from the Mass Education Group, and 2 from the Boy Scout Training Group. The significance of convening this conference can be summarized in three points: 1) It is hoped that the conference proposals will be practical and feasible, so as to avoid the shortcomings of previous conferences where discussions did not lead to action. The most practical areas in Jiangxi are bandit-affected area education and mass education. We must spend less money and work harder. Those who are literate should have the obligation to teach those who are illiterate, and those who are illiterate should have the obligation to become literate. 2) It is hoped that the conference participants will concentrate their time, talent, and ideas for discussion. 3) It is hoped that the conference participants will work together to improve. Whether education is well-managed in the future is entirely the responsibility of everyone. It is hoped that everyone will have the greatest awareness and make sacrifices and efforts, so that there is hope for educational improvement. Next, representatives of Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, Liu Jiashu of the Provincial Party Headquarters, and Wu Jiantao of the Provincial Government gave instructions. Finally, representatives of the members gave speeches and the meeting adjourned.

Fifth Broadcast of National Salvation Propaganda by the University Federation 176

In the first set, Zheng took an early lead of 5-3, but then it became 5-5, and he finally won 7-5. In the second set, Zheng took an early lead of 4-1, then it became 4-3 and 5-3, Smith then tied the score at 5-5, Zheng won again 7-5. Smith was never able to take the lead in any game or achieve an equal score. In the third set, Zheng's cross-court shots were able to be used with ease. The ball was close to the sideline, and the speed was as fast as an arrow. Smith was unable to defend himself and was exhausted, resulting in his inability to come up with a plan. Zheng won 6-0, which was easy.
